King of England's Broadcast Address: Hoping for World Peace, Mutual Understanding, and Prosperity for the British People 24

London: This afternoon, King Edward delivered an address to the people at home and abroad from the broadcasting studio. At four o'clock in the afternoon, after the radio station broadcast national music, the King spoke, hoping for world peace and mutual understanding, as well as prosperity and happiness for the British people. This was Edward's 76th speech on the radio, but his first as King. Countless people in Britain and around the world listened to his speech. The number of listeners was unprecedented. According to reports from various places, the King's speech was heard exceptionally clearly. According to a Reuters dispatch from Cape Town, except for occasional pauses, the entire Union of South Africa heard his speech without any ambiguity. The same was true in the United States, India, Australia, Canada, European countries, and South America. Queen Mary was at Buckingham Palace, and Prime Minister Baldwin was at Chequers, both listening quietly via wireless. The King said, "It is a long-standing tradition in our country that a new monarch must address the people. Today, with the development of science, I am able to use the wireless to speak to my people, which is more intimate than sending a written message. This is not something I have initiated. In the past few years, my father has used the wireless to deliver a Christmas message to the public. Only two months ago, my father broadcast his Christmas message, and I believe many of my people still hear his voice in their ears. My father reigned for twenty-five years, and during this long period, many extraordinary changes have occurred. Great hardships and complex problems have been encountered by all. My father was always diligent in his duties, always thinking of the happiness of the people under his jurisdiction and protection, setting a good example for us. In times of difficulty, my father's calmness and trust in all the people helped to alleviate the situation. He shared the joys and sorrows of the people. I know that the autonomy must extend to India and the colonies, and the crown, which is a symbol of the unity of many places and peoples, is increasingly strengthened by their loyalty, which is due to their love and respect for my father. I feel that my father's passing is not only a great grief for my mother and my brothers, but also a personal loss for the general public of the British Empire. I now extend my respects as Emperor to the princes and people of India. Your expressions of mourning for the national mourning and your expressions of loyalty to the new Emperor are deeply appreciated. The connection between the British and the Indians, both in peacetime and in wartime, has a long history and can be regarded as an honor. The sacred trust of maintaining and strengthening this connection, as exemplified by Queen Victoria, Edward VII, and George V, is now passed on to me as their successor. My mother, my family, and myself are deeply moved by the sincere expressions of mourning that have come from all parts of the world. The large number of people who paid their respects at my father's funeral and the many letters and telegrams of condolence from home and abroad are something we will never forget. My father's great character was admired by the whole world. His popularity cannot be seen in empty words. My father's many years of diligent service were rewarded with the people's love and loyalty, as can be seen during the celebration of the 25th anniversary of his reign last year. My father was delighted to witness this before his death. Inheriting the legacy of my predecessors, I now bear this responsibility. I am the Prince of Wales, whom you all know. During the war and after the war, I had the opportunity to interact with people from all over the world in various circumstances. I now speak as the King of England, but I am still the person who has made friends with the people, and I will always be committed to continuing to promote human happiness. I wish for the future to bring peace and understanding to the world, and prosperity and happiness to the people of England. I also wish that we will not fail in our duties." (1st Day Reuters Dispatch)

German Propaganda Minister's Speech: Germany's Economic Life Destroyed by the Treaty of Versailles 25

Leipzig, Germany: The Clean Market here opened today. The ceremony was presided over by Propaganda Minister Goebbels, who delivered a speech stating: "The Treaty of Versailles deprived Germany of its sources of raw materials and seized the capital it had accumulated, which was enough to destroy Germany's economic life. Those who negotiated at the Versailles Peace Conference all had one goal in mind: 'Germany will become weaker day by day, while other countries will prosper day by day.' Goebbels then described the worldwide economic panic in recent years, saying, "The reason for this is none other than the uneven distribution of raw materials, the reversal of the principles of trade, the confusion and mistakes of capitalists, the instability of currency, and the violation of the natural order in the accounting system. In short, the circulation of huge amounts of gold is not enough to create national happiness. For example, the United States now has gold worth 24,600,000,000 yuan, almost half of the world's gold reserves. But even with so much gold, is the welfare of the United States better than that of other countries? The answer is no. The United States has a total of nine million unemployed people, which shows that the United States is still in a state of calamity. In Germany, since the National Socialist Party came to power, the number of unemployed people has decreased by five million. Recently, in the industrial sector, three new substitutes have been invented: artificial oil (i.e., petroleum spirit), artificial fibers, and artificial rubber. Among them, if the manufacturing plan for artificial fibers is fully realized, Germany's current imports of fibers can be reduced by 25%." (1st Day Havas Dispatch)

Cause of Tokyo Incident: Defects in Social Organization; War Minister Kawashima Advises Saionji; Foreign Ministry Also Says It is an Internal Affair 26

Tokyo: War Minister Kawashima is determined to actively advise Saionji to form a national unity cabinet, and is determined to devote all his efforts to thoroughly suppress the military, so as to avoid any more unfortunate incidents. The long-term and immediate causes of this incident lie in the defects of the social organization and the accumulation of malpractices in the political world for many years, which is well known to everyone. Therefore, those who are in charge of the regime should carefully consider the situation and implement politics that conform to the extraordinary times, so as to meet the expectations of the people. (2nd Day Domei Dispatch)

Tokyo: A Foreign Ministry spokesman told foreign journalists today that Japan's foreign policy will not change. No matter how the cabinet changes, foreign policy will continue. The incident on Wednesday arose from internal problems and has nothing to do with the country's foreign policy. This can be seen from the fact that the Foreign Ministry was not disturbed during the incident. (2nd Day Reuters Dispatch)

Tokyo: All cabinet members gathered at the Imperial Household Ministry before 10:00 a.m. today to exchange information and hold cordial talks. In addition, privy councilors met with the Emperor separately to report on the situation. The first Privy Council meeting since the outbreak of the incident was held at 1:00 p.m. All cabinet members and army and navy officers were present. It is reported that the Emperor will also attend today's important meeting in person. (2nd Day Dentsu Dispatch)

Saionji Arrives in Tokyo; Consults with Senior Statesmen on Selection of Cabinet Members 27

Tokyo: In view of the seriousness of the situation, Duke Saionji, upon arriving in Tokyo, immediately visited the Emperor and stayed at the Imperial Household Ministry. Count Makino also arrived in Tokyo on the afternoon of the 2nd. Count Kiyoura is still in Atami, but may arrive in Tokyo on the 3rd. Privy Councilor Iki and Minister of the Imperial Household Yuasa are both at the Imperial Household Ministry. Baron Wakatsuki is also in Tokyo. All these senior statesmen will gather in Tokyo in the next two days. During his stay in Tokyo, Saionji will temporarily reside at the Imperial Household Ministry in the Imperial Palace. After responding to the Emperor's inquiries, he will convene a meeting of senior statesmen there. (2nd Day Domei News Agency Dispatch)

Tokyo: Duke Saionji arrived here at 3:25 p.m. today and immediately entered the palace. Privy Council Ministers and Cabinet members greeted him at the palace gate. Duke Saionji is currently staying in the palace. The Emperor will consult him on the selection of a new Lord Keeper of the Privy Seal. The previous Lord Keeper of the Privy Seal, Viscount Saito, was killed by mutinous soldiers on Wednesday. This position is very important and should not be left vacant for long, as the Lord Keeper of the Privy Seal is the liaison between the Emperor and the government. Duke Saionji will, as usual, recommend candidates for the new Prime Minister, but due to the complex situation, it will take several days to make a decision. He will convene a meeting of Count Makino, Count Kiyoura, Baron Iki, Baron Wakatsuki, Minister of the Imperial Household Yuasa, and the current Prime Minister Okada to discuss this matter. Reports say that the new cabinet will be a cabinet of capable people, but without Fascist elements. Before appointing a new Prime Minister, the Lord Keeper of the Privy Seal will be selected first. (2nd Day Reuters Dispatch)

Okitsu: Duke Saionji, accompanied by his adopted son Hachiro, Kumao Harada, Kojuro Nakagawa, and other attendants, arrived in Shizuoka at 11:30 a.m. this morning. He took a train to Tokyo at 12:30 p.m. and is scheduled to arrive in Tokyo at 3:30 p.m. If he is received by the Emperor and asked about the formation of a cabinet, he will naturally seek the opinions of the military and senior statesmen such as Kiyoura, Makino, and Wakatsuki. In order to deeply understand the current situation, he will break with tradition and solicit the opinions of promising newcomers in a wide range for reference. It is now widely rumored that the following people are candidates to succeed the cabinet: Privy Councilor and Army General Kawai Masao, Privy Council Chairman Hiranuma Kiichirō, President of the House of Peers Konoe Fumimaro, Army General Araki Sadao, Count Kiyoura Keigo, and Baron Yamamoto Tatsuo. (2nd Day Domei Dispatch)

Army and Navy Advocate Forming a National Unity Cabinet; The Prime Minister's Task Should Not Be Chosen by the Military 28

Tokyo: The Army authorities held a headquarters meeting at 4:00 p.m. on the 1st. War Minister Kawashima, Director-General of Military Affairs Kozō, Director of Military Affairs Imai, Director of Personnel Kokyū, Director of Maintenance Yamakyo, Director of Accounting Hirate, and Director of Legal Affairs Ōyama attended. They exchanged important opinions on how to deal with the current situation and thoroughly suppress the military for five hours. The meeting adjourned at 9:00 p.m. Director of Military Affairs Imai immediately went to the Kudan Kaikosha to visit the military councilors and report on the meeting. Then, the highest headquarters, based on this report, deliberated until late at night. As a result, regarding the formation of a cabinet, if Duke Saionji seeks the opinion of the military, it was decided to answer with: 1. Thoroughly implement the suppression of the military, 2. Realize a powerful and capable national unity cabinet. (2nd Day Domei Dispatch)

Tokyo: The Army side, in view of the seriousness of this incident, hopes that the person to succeed as Prime Minister will meet the following objectives: 1. Regarding the fundamental policy of national policy, 2. Thoroughly correct the National Army. Regarding this matter, the Army Ministry and the General Staff Headquarters should conduct important deliberations and achieve results. The Army hopes that the next cabinet will thoroughly implement various policies and form a truly powerful national unity cabinet. Its leader does not necessarily have to be an elder or an established politician, nor a general in the army or navy. New talents must be promoted. War Minister Kawashima will open the general intentions of the military when Duke Saionji seeks his opinion. (2nd Day Domei News Agency Dispatch)

Tokyo: According to the opinions of senior Navy officials, the new cabinet must have the power to handle the aftermath of the major events to come, deal with the current situation, break the current deadlock in Japan, and establish a fundamental national policy. The new cabinet should strengthen national defense in the face of the extraordinary international situation, and fundamentally reform domestic affairs. Its personnel should be selected from outside the army and navy, and a powerful national unity cabinet should be formed. (2nd Day Domei Dispatch)

Tokyo: On the 29th, the Army authorities ordered the dismissal of the instigating officers of the riot incident from their posts. The Imperial Household Ministry also issued an order on the same day, ordering the return of their ranks. (2nd Day Nichiren Dispatch)

Tokyo: Five police officers were killed while performing their duties during the incident on Wednesday. The public expressed deep sympathy for them, and 5,000 yuan has been donated to provide for their families. (2nd Day Reuters Dispatch)

Tokyo: The regular March personnel changes in the Army were internally ordered last month, and were scheduled to be formally ordered on the 2nd of this month. However, due to the incident, the contents have been revised, so the order has been temporarily postponed. (2nd Day Domei Dispatch)

Financial Circles Oppose a Fascist Cabinet To Avoid Financial Chaos 29

Tokyo: Machida, the Minister of Commerce currently holding the position of Finance Minister, told reporters today that the candidate for the new Prime Minister will be selected in two or three days. He believes that the new cabinet will be a national unity cabinet, representing various political parties and other forces. At the same time, leaders of the economic and financial circles have expressed their opinion that the new cabinet must not be of a Fascist nature. (2nd Day Reuters Dispatch)

Tokyo: On the day of the end of the incident, the financial and economic circles are paying close attention to the future trends and who will be recommended as the leader of the next cabinet. Because the financial circles lost Finance Minister Takahashi, a pillar, due to this incident, there are not a few people who are quite concerned about whether the method of gradually reducing public debt and the sound financial policy will be adhered to in the future. In the event of any shake-up, the impact on the general financial circles is a matter of concern. Therefore, there is a strong desire for the leader of the next cabinet not to break this iron rule. Although the financial circles hope to build a national unity and cooperative cabinet, its power must first be able to deal with the current situation. However, if the current economic structure is merely modified, there is a fear that this will cause drastic changes in the entire finances, and even plunge the economic world into extreme chaos. It is believed that it is imperative to avoid the emergence of such a cabinet in the future. (1st Day Domei News Agency Dispatch)

Statement of the Seiyukai: Striving for Constitutional Politics 30

Tokyo: The Seiyukai held an extraordinary executive meeting at its headquarters at 11:00 a.m. on the 2nd and passed the following statement: "This incident is an unprecedentedly unfortunate case. Looking back on the duty of subjects, we are terrified and do not know what to do. However, the responsibility for this situation should be made clear, and it goes without saying that the reality of the suppression should be resolutely demonstrated at this time, and the reality of reform should be carried out by fundamentally reviewing politics, economy, and everything else. This is a matter of utmost urgency. Our party must clarify the great cause of the founding of the nation, take the spirit of the founding of the party as the law, uphold constitutional politics, and strive to promote the reality of a new public and private life. At the same time, the entire nation should cooperate and unite, promote the essence of the national polity, and sincerely make faithful efforts for constitutional politics. This is what we earnestly hope for." (2nd Day Domei Dispatch)

Okada's Escape: First Hidden in a Large Iron Box, Later Concealed in His Brother-in-Law's Coffin; Rebel Troops Opposed Araki's Cabinet Formation 31

(Foreign Press) According to a report in the Shanghai-based North-China Daily News, the following detailed account of the Tokyo Incident was obtained via wireless telegraph yesterday:

Premier Okada's escape from death is said to be due to his brother-in-law, Colonel Matsuo, intentionally concealing him and voluntarily sacrificing himself. Matsuo was well aware that the rebel soldiers were unable to distinguish between the two men's faces and movements. The Premier himself hid in a large steel cabinet, with servants in the house constantly informing him of the situation outside. When family and friends remaining in the private residence requested permission to move the remains, the rebels' mistake was immediately discovered. Fortunately, Premier Okada's hiding place was known to his family and friends, and he was able to conceal himself in his brother-in-law's coffin, which was then transported out of the danger zone. The rebel soldiers did not create any difficulty when the coffin was carried out, as they were unaware that the person they had killed was not Okada himself. News of Okada's arrival at the private residence did not leak out until after the rebel soldiers had surrendered.

After receiving the details of the incident in Shanghai yesterday, it became clear that the number of people killed and injured in the incident was actually higher than reported in the Tokyo dispatches of various newspapers. It is said that the total number of deaths exceeded one hundred, many of whom were male and female servants in the private residences of the ministers who were attacked.

It is reported that the Tokyo incident was launched before dawn. The original participants were all troops from the First Division. They were fully armed, carrying several machine guns and many boxes of hand grenades. They entered the city in multiple freight trucks. After entering the city, each truck immediately dispersed in different directions. Two or three of them went to the residences of various cabinet members, and several others drove to Count Makino's villa and Duke Saionji's private residence in Shizuoka.

The headquarters of the Imperial Capital Police and the Tokyo Military Police were also among the places the rebel soldiers planned to occupy immediately, in order to avoid resistance. The police were generally unarmed, but the military police and specially armed police stationed at various official residences did open fire to resist the attacking rebel soldiers. Although it is difficult to obtain accurate information on this point, there was at least one street battle. As a result, one person on each side died. At the same time, the guards at the residence of Watanabe, the Director-General of Education, also fired at the approaching freight trucks. One rebel soldier immediately fell to the ground and died. The machine guns then began to operate. After a few minutes, the wooden walls of Watanabe's residence were covered with bullet marks. Watanabe himself, hearing the first gunshot, rushed downstairs and stood on the steps outside the door, where he was seen by the rebel soldiers and immediately shot dead.

The guards at Saito's residence put up some resistance, but were quickly overcome. The rebel soldiers then rushed inside. It is said that they found Saito in the bedroom and stabbed him to death with bayonets. The body of this elderly statesman had thirty bayonet wounds, which shows how many people were involved in the attack. Saito's wife was also injured. Finance Minister Takahashi was shot and died instantly. However, his death was not announced until Thursday afternoon, and was attributed to injuries, apparently to avoid financial panic.

Grand Chamberlain Suzuki was the only victim who lived for several hours. He also passed away that afternoon, having suffered multiple gunshot wounds.

The rebel soldiers' attacks on Makino and Saionji were fortunately delayed by a moment, and they were unable to achieve their goals. A few minutes before the rebel soldiers arrived by car, both men received telephone warnings, urging them to flee. Duke Saionji was also protected by the Shizuoka police and left in a fast car. Makino was rescued by a worker who hid him in a nearby small mountain. By the time the rebel soldiers arrived, Makino was long gone. Disappointed, the rebel soldiers bombarded his villa with machine guns and bombs, and then burned it down to vent their anger.

By the time the residents of Tokyo woke up the next morning (as there was no disturbance except in the government center and near various official residences), the city was completely in the hands of the rebel soldiers. The telephone exchange was also occupied. Except for the telephone lines between Tokyo and Osaka and Kobe, all other lines were blocked. The Tokyo Asahi Shimbun newspaper was also attacked by the rebel soldiers, who destroyed the newspaper's new equipment. It is also reported that the factory of the Mainichi Shimbun newspaper was also destroyed by them. Each newspaper office was guarded by a machine gun squad. Apart from announcements released by the rebel soldiers, no other news was allowed to be published.

The Ministry of the Army was occupied, and the staff of the General Staff who were on duty at the time were imprisoned. Only lower-level personnel were present in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and they were also arrested at that time.

Soldiers were stationed near the residences of Interior Minister Goto and Acting Finance Minister Machida. Although these two men had nothing to do with the incident, the rebel soldiers apparently had some use for them.

When the incident began, there were only nine hundred rebel soldiers attacking various locations. By early morning, the 1st and 3rd Regiments and the Chiba Artillery Regiment had joined them. In the afternoon, the Kure 29th Regiment, the Akabane Regiment, and other units also cooperated with the rebel soldiers, bringing their total number to 2,400. By evening, it had increased to 3,000. The Chiba Air Corps stood by and watched. Three cruisers from Yokosuka arrived in Tokyo Bay, and several platoons of naval soldiers entered the port and landed.

The attitude of the landing sailors at the time caused a great deal of speculation. Initially, it was thought that they intended to pacify the entire city, but Fleet Admiral Prince Fushimi stayed in the palace all day. The only order received by the fleet was to avoid conflict with the rebel soldiers. The soldiers of the First Division, under the guidance of their divisional commander, Horinouchi, were busy erecting barbed wire obstacles near the Imperial Palace. Those who attended the morning meeting in the palace included Generals Araki, Kawashima, and Mazaki. As a result, they proposed terms to the rebel soldiers, intending to appoint Araki to form a new cabinet. Unexpectedly, this proposal was rejected by the rebel soldiers, who issued a kind of ultimatum, signed by Captain Ezaki, which stated roughly: "We demand the complete overthrow of the government, the elders, the senior officials, and the politicians, as well as the corrupt commercial interests, who seek to profit from the nation's difficulties. Unless our demands are completely met, we will continue to fight against the right-wing elements in the army and eliminate the capitalists."

This ultimatum can be seen as expressing the extreme faction in the army's opposition to industrialists. According to the opinion of some people, since Japanese soldiers receive only seven sen in pay each day, it is customary to issue notices to the people living near the barracks, requesting donations so that the soldiers can occasionally enjoy a few luxuries. The poor people dare not refuse such donations, and often contribute as much as they can. The wealthier people, although able to donate, often refuse.

What is noteworthy about this matter is Premier Okada's narrow escape from assassination, and the sudden re-emergence of Admiral Kato. We should recall that during the London Naval Conference, Okada was a senior naval officer and chief technical representative who participated in the conference. Okada's efforts were largely responsible for the conclusion of the commercial agreement. When Okada returned to the country, Kato was angered by his acceptance of the 5:5:3 ratio, and immediately resigned.

After an all-night meeting, the princes and military councilors decided to declare martial law at four o'clock in the morning. However, it was practically useless, as the rebel soldiers still guarded the official residences, and the Ministry of the Army and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs were still unable to resume work. Everything was still under the absolute control of the rebel soldiers, who insisted that their original demands be completely accepted.

The special editions of the newspapers and the special wireless dispatches on Thursday morning still contained very little news. The government ordered the people to remain calm and not to believe rumors. It is said that the reason for the declaration of martial law was partly to maintain public order in Tokyo, and partly to prevent radicals from taking the opportunity to cause trouble. General Kashii has now been appointed to take full responsibility for martial law. Some rebel soldiers had withdrawn from one or two places, but reappeared there in the afternoon. The Nobles Club was also one of the places that had been occupied. The current reality is that Tokyo has increasingly no troops ready to fight the rebel soldiers.

Candidates for the Next Army Minister: General Abe and Lieutenant General Sugiyama Are Promising 32

In order to restore the prestige of the national army and promote the true unity and consolidation of the national army, he will recommend a person of both character and insight as the successor to the Army Minister. To guide the national army in this extraordinary period, it must be someone with real strength. He is also seeking the opinions of General Kawai and other important figures, hoping for a comprehensive solution. Naval Conference: Britain is Agile, Having Concluded an Agreement with the United States and France, and Now Seeking Separate Agreements with Germany and Russia 33

London - Britain has suggested to Germany that in addition to the naval treaty signed by Britain, France, and the United States, a separate Anglo-German naval agreement be concluded. Regarding this matter, German Embassy Counselor Bismarck submitted a response to British Foreign Secretary Eden last Saturday, stating that Germany is prepared to sign a bilateral agreement. According to this agency's reporter, the Anglo-German naval agreement will be based on the principles contained in the British, French, and American naval treaty. In the British, French, and American treaty, there are still some technical details that are unresolved. Once the final agreement is reached, Britain will submit a copy to Germany. If Germany expresses approval of the terms of this agreement, then Britain and Germany can sign the agreement. In addition, after the British, French, and American naval agreement is signed, Britain and Russia should also sign a naval agreement, just as Britain and Germany have done. As for inviting Soviet Russia to participate in the British, French, and American agreement, Britain has never considered it. Up to this point, it has not taken any action with the Soviet Russian government, only informing the Soviet Russian government of the progress of the naval conference. (2nd, Havas News)

London - Recently, Britain proposed that Britain and Germany sign a separate bilateral naval agreement in addition to the future British, French, and American naval treaty. The German ambassador to Britain, Heesch, was instructed by his government to request instructions. According to this agency's reporter, Ambassador Heesch has received instructions from his government, approving this proposal, but with the condition that the construction of warships between 10,000-ton cruisers and 20,000-ton battleships (the tonnage of battleships is a minimum of 20,000 tons) be prohibited. The French delegation, having received instructions from their government yesterday, which provided guidance on the issue of signing the British, French, and American treaty, has decided to discuss the contents of these instructions this morning, and then meet with the British and American delegations to select a date for convening the naval conference to discuss the final terms of the three-nation treaty. (2nd, Havas News)

The United States Will Build New Warships: Chairman of the House Naval Affairs Committee Expresses 34

Washington - Chairman Vincent of the House Naval Affairs Committee hinted today that the United States Navy may increase the construction of new battleships. He said that until the results of the London Naval Conference are known, the committee does not want to take any action on the proposal to allow the repair of fourteen warships and the modernization of six warships. If the lifespan of battleships is not extended by the Naval Conference, then the United States is willing to build new ships to replace old ships, rather than repairing or modernizing the old ships. (1st, Reuters)

Three South Pacific Islands: Britain Acknowledges U.S. Occupation; Still Uninhabited 35

London - The British Foreign Office today acknowledged that Howland Island, Jarvis Island, and Baker Island in the South Pacific have been occupied by the United States. According to a spokesman for the Foreign Office, it is not very clear to which country these three islands should belong, but we believe that Britain should have the right to occupy them. However, if the United States has formally incorporated them into its own territory, then Britain is not willing to compete with it. These three islands were formerly leased by Britain to an Australian company, but it is reported that they are still uninhabited and undeveloped. (1st, Kokumin News)

Belgian House of Representatives Studies the State of German Armaments; Radek Discusses the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty 36

Brussels - The House of Representatives' Defense Committee, which previously planned to submit a report on the issue of the demilitarized zone of the Rhineland, appointed Committee Member Treppe as the drafter. Treppe has now completed the draft, which states in part that although Germany has not sent national defense forces into the demilitarized zone, there are more than 30,000 police officers stationed in the area, all stationed in military camps and fully armed (the Versailles Treaty only allows a police force of 8,440). In addition, there are various informal military organizations, the number of which is difficult to determine. Members of the forced labor corps serve for six months, and are constantly replaced, so their number is also difficult to ascertain. Finally, Treppe mentioned the issue of Germany attacking Belgium in the event of war, saying that some people are concerned that Germany will pass through the Netherlands to invade Belgium, but the Belgian General Staff has been studying methods of prevention for more than a year. (1st, Havas News) Radek on Hitler in Izvestia

Moscow - Radek discussed Hitler's conversation with a reporter from Le Journal in Izvestia. "The Franco-Soviet pact, regardless of Hitler's threats and the weeping of his representatives in France, was approved by the Chamber of Deputies. The Democratic Republic of France is unwilling to be subdued by Hitler and his representatives in France, but this pact has not yet been approved by the Senate. The opponents of the Franco-Soviet pact will make a final effort to delay the approval of the pact. 'Fischer' personally came forward to compromise with the French right-wing, and began to describe inaccurate facts, saying that when the Ruhr was occupied, he wrote 'My Struggle' in prison." Hitler hopes that his French friends will conceal from the French people the various declarations he made between 1925 and 1932, promising the open letter to Papen on October 21, 1922. In this letter, he called on Germany to secretly expand its armaments as a policy to counter France, relying on this to unite with Britain and Italy to resist France. This was not during the occupation of the Ruhr, but in the autumn of 1932, on the eve of his assumption of power. Hitler advocated Germany uniting with Italy and Britain to resist France. Since Hitler came to power, he has been committed to establishing a German-Italian bloc to resist France, but due to the conflict between Italy and Germany over Austrian policy, and Britain's pursuit of peace, this effort to establish an anti-French bloc has not yet succeeded. Therefore, Hitler had to send his affections to France, while simultaneously attacking the Franco-Polish alliance, wooing France's ally Czechoslovakia, and weakening France's alliance with Yugoslavia, isolating France and causing it to succumb. Hitler vaguely threatened that the Franco-Soviet treaty created a 'new environment', repeatedly reversed himself, slandered the Soviet Union, and warned France to beware of the Soviet Union. Hitler disregards the inevitable trend of international relations. He will have no right to complain. As we have declared, Hitler has no revolutionary ideas in his mind, and no ideas at all, only the ideas of a small shopkeeper. But we must admit that in terms of explosion and disaster, no one can compare with the Hitler regime. His party representatives and we all know this. With his unparalleled crudeness, his remarks to France are like those of Bismarck before Sedan, or Wilhelm II before the First World War. Only those who have lost their minds, lost all their balance, and think that others do not know their actual position can be so unrestrained. We firmly believe that the result of Hitler's remarks will be the opposite of what he expects. In this conversation, Hitler treats France as if it were a defeated country, or a country that must fear him, but the reality is not so. France is not a weak country. It hopes for peace, but does not expect to be bound by others. We can assert that Hitler and his representatives in France will surely understand this in the future. The sooner they realize this, the wider the road to peace will be. History tells us that Caesar and arrogant monarchs also had the same great self-confidence, but when they saw what the Germans call 'the stick over the dog's head', they also humbled themselves. History tells us that there are also those who refuse to yield, but for those suffering from Caesar's mental disorder, history will surely make them conform." (1st, TASS)

Vast US Public Debt 37

Washington learned today that after the Treasury Department raised $1,809,000,000 in debt on March 15, the US public debt reached an unprecedented amount of $31,300,000,000. It is reported that the Treasury Department must first issue $1,250,000,000 in new bonds to absorb cash. The bonds will be of two types: one is a 2.75% bond maturing in March 1951, totaling $650,000,000, but the government has the right to redeem it in March 1948; the other is a 1.5% bond maturing in March 1941, totaling $600,000,000. The cash received will be allocated $450,000,000 to pay off short-term debt due on March 16. Therefore, after offsetting the new and old debts, the net new debt is $800,000,000. This amount will be included in the Treasury's cash reserve to be used for relief efforts, rural assistance, and pensions for veterans. It is expected that after the Treasury Department obtains this new debt, plus the revenue from the increased income tax, it can obtain more than $2,000,000,000 in working capital. As for the Treasury bonds of $559,000,000 due on April 15, new bonds will be issued again at that time to raise funds to repay them. (2nd, Reuters)

Washington - The Treasury Department will issue two new public bonds tomorrow, one with a total value of $650 million, with an interest rate of 2.75%, repayable in 12 to 15 years, and the other with a total value of $600 million, with an interest rate of 1.25%, repayable in 5 years. These two public bonds are the largest in terms of amount since the issuance of the Victory Bonds of 1919. After being listed tomorrow, they will bring the national debt to a new record of $31,300,000,000. In addition, in order to recover the public debt due in mid-April, the Treasury Department also plans to issue new public bonds of $558,819,000 with an interest rate of 2.875% to swap for the old debt. (1st, Kokumin News)

Washington - According to well-informed sources here today, Roosevelt must raise a huge sum of $1,137,000,000 to pay for veterans' allowances and implement the new agricultural bill. As a result, a new manufacturing tax bill may be redrafted. At the same time, the inflationists in both houses, seeing the necessity of this next expenditure, are also greatly active in the hope of redrafting a method for further inflating the currency. The most radical of the currency inflation plans is the rural mortgage refinancing bill proposed by Flansburgh and Langley. Those who support this bill are all trying to draw attention to it before the national conventions of the Republican and Democratic parties are held. Therefore, the issue of currency inflation is something that both the Republican and Democratic parties cannot help but determine their attitude towards. (1st, Kokumin News)

Washington - Secretary of Agriculture Wallace, in order to protect the interests of the flour industry in the Northwestern states, has decided to exercise his power to subsidize the export of flour with 30% of the tariff revenue. According to Wallace, with this subsidy, the Northwestern region can export 333,000 barrels of flour to the Philippines. However, the calculation of this subsidy will be based daily on the difference between the production cost of American flour and the market price of flour in the Philippines. Wallace also said that before 1930, the United States supplied 83% of the total flour consumption in the Philippines, but at present, the sales of American flour in the Philippines have fallen to less than 10%. According to well-informed sources, after the flour export subsidy is implemented, subsidies for the export of general agricultural products may also begin. (1st, Kokumin News)

League of Nations Eighteen-Nation Committee Meeting: Increased Sanctions Against Italy Postponed; Anglo-French Foreign Ministers Agree After Arriving in Geneva: Italy to Leverage Military Victory to Promote Peace 39

Geneva – During the Eighteen-Nation Committee meeting this afternoon, British Foreign Secretary Eden stated that the British government had reviewed the Experts Committee report. If other countries agree to implement an oil embargo, the British government will support its implementation. (Reuters, 2nd) This morning, British Foreign Secretary Eden held talks with French Foreign Minister Flandin and Minister without Portfolio Pengcou. It is generally understood that they agreed to postpone discussion of increased sanctions against Italy in the League of Nations Eighteen-Nation Subcommittee, to facilitate negotiations and seek a solution to the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. Regarding this, the British and French authorities have reached an agreement with the subcommittee chairman, Vasconcelos, so that only the second part of the original agenda (i.e., reviewing the report of the Sanctions Implementation Experts Committee) will be discussed at the subcommittee meeting today, while the first part (i.e., increased sanctions against Italy) will be postponed. (Havas, 2nd)

Paris – The League of Nations Eighteen-Nation Subcommittee is scheduled to meet today. The method of embargoing oil, which is of most general concern, is about to be implemented. According to speculation by the correspondent of the "Little Daily" stationed in Geneva, both the Soviet Union and Romania are currently unwilling to abandon their commercial interests. Therefore, the embargo measure is unlikely to be implemented, as both countries deeply fear that once the embargo is implemented, Italy will inevitably purchase the oil it needs from the United States, and the Italian market will be monopolized by American oil merchants, excluding the two countries. According to well-informed sources, since the oil embargo is impractical, the Eighteen-Nation Subcommittee may seek other ways to compensate, such as prohibiting Italian ships from entering ports belonging to League of Nations member states. Another approach being considered by people in the United Kingdom and Scandinavian countries is to provide financial assistance to the invaded country. "Business Report" states that although Italy is subject to sanctions and goods cannot be exported, the practice of smuggling goods out of the country via Switzerland, Germany, Austria, and Hungary has not disappeared. Efforts are now being made to curb this, so that there will be no more smuggling. Geneva believes that if this method is actually implemented, it will increase the effectiveness of the sanctions. (Havas, 2nd)

Paris – After arriving in Geneva this morning, British Foreign Secretary Eden will first hold talks with French Foreign Minister Flandin. According to observations by the diplomatic correspondent of "Business Report", this conversation is the most important event of the current session of the League of Nations Eighteen-Nation Subcommittee, as the two will discuss the following five issues: the possibility of peace between Italy and Ethiopia; what methods can be used to make Germany return to the League of Nations; after the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty is approved by the French Senate and Chamber of Deputies, what attitude should the UK and France take if Germany requests a conference of the signatory countries of the Locarno Treaty; what attitude should the UK and France take if Germany re-fortifies the demilitarized zone in the Rhineland; and various issues regarding the naval conference. (Havas, 2nd)

Geneva – The recent victories of the Italian army in northern Ethiopia are considered important by people at the League of Nations. It is expected that the Italian government will take advantage of this opportunity to initiate diplomatic moves to resolve the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. As for the League of Nations Eighteen-Nation Subcommittee, which was originally scheduled to meet today to discuss increased sanctions against Italy, it is now learned that the subcommittee chairman, Vasconcelos, at the request of British Foreign Secretary Eden and French Foreign Minister Flandin, has decided to postpone the discussion of increased sanctions against Italy, so that representatives of the countries concerned can determine their attitude and await a clear expression of intent from the Italian government. (Havas, 2nd)

Rome – As the League of Nations Administrative Council is about to meet to discuss increased sanctions against Italy, the Italian government has today prepared to redefine its foreign policy. If the League of Nations expands economic sanctions, Italy may withdraw from the League of Nations and abolish the Locarno Treaty. Reliable sources predict that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will turn to Germany and other countries that do not participate in the sanctions, and will seek to conclude defensive treaties on economic and diplomatic matters to cope with the oil embargo. At the same time, the whole country is ecstatic because General Badoglio won a great victory on the northern front in Ethiopia on the 14th anniversary of the First Battle of Adwa. Today, the Italian King and Mussolini personally led 50,000 Roman residents to the Tomb of the Unknown Soldier for a solemn military parade. Afterwards, citizens marched through the streets, praising the achievements of the Italian King and Mussolini. Mussolini frequently returned their greetings, even stopping work for nine minutes. (National Telegram, 1st)

Geneva – As far as our correspondent knows, although Italy's war against Ethiopia is very successful, British Foreign Secretary Eden still supports increased sanctions against Italy and continues to implement the principles contained in the League of Nations Covenant. In addition, most representatives agree with the British representative's expression of surprise and displeasure at Italy's large-scale military operations and widespread propaganda of Italian military victories on the eve of the meeting of the Eighteen-Nation Subcommittee. (Havas, 2nd)

Italian Commander-in-Chief Announces: Ethiopian Army on the Northern Front Completely Defeated; Ethiopian Emperor Plans a Desperate Last Stand 40

Tigre Province Front, Ethiopia – General Badoglio, High Commissioner for East Africa and Commander-in-Chief of the Italian Army, recently told reporters at the General Headquarters, "The Ethiopian army on the northern front has now been completely defeated. This is a joyous event. Its Second Army has been annihilated by our army. In the blink of an eye, its Third Army will also be destroyed. From then on, the Ethiopian army on the northern front can be cleared. At this moment, the remaining enemies, forgetting themselves, disregarding everything, are eager to cross the Geva River and flee back to their hometowns, abandoning all their guns and ammunition along the way, so that those who see them do not recognize them as soldiers, but think they are villagers," etc. According to our correspondent, the troops of Ethiopian Army Minister General Muluguetae and General Gassa, commander-in-chief of the northern front, have retreated after Tombien. Therefore, this battle can be said to have decided the outcome of the war. Moreover, the Tombien area is undulating with hills and rugged terrain, which is a natural barrier, but the Italian army captured it in one fell swoop, which shows that Ethiopia is really difficult to resist under large-scale military operations. Now the morale of the Ethiopian army is low, and the defeated army is scattered and cannot be reorganized. The soldiers have all fled back to their hometowns, and there are no reserve troops to continue fighting. It is said that when the battle of Tombien was about to end, the Ethiopian emperor planned to make a desperate last stand, personally leading the Guards northward from the city of Taixi, hoping to rescue General Muluguetae or attack the rear of the Italian Third Army (which was attacking the troops of General Gassa from the side at that time). However, he failed to arrive in time. When he reached the vicinity of Gualan, he was ambushed by the Italian army and suffered heavy losses, so he had to lead his troops to retreat. (Havas, 1st)

Asmara – According to a dispatch from Holm, special correspondent for Reuters in the central part of the Italian army on the northern front, after suffering the greatest defeat of his life, General Gassa is now leading the remnants to flee southwest. Gassa's 40,000 troops have been divided into several groups and are fleeing in all directions. After Gassa withdrew his troops from Mount Uok on February 28, he attacked again yesterday. The two sides fought fiercely for a long time. The Ethiopian army, feeling surrounded by two Italian columns, desperately tried to break through the Nawo Pass, but was blocked by the Italian army, and then fled in confusion. It is now believed that General Gassa's defeat will have a major impact on the internal situation in Ethiopia, because Gassa is known as the "Elder of Northern Ethiopia" and is wealthier than the Ethiopian King. His prestige is unmatched by any politician in Ethiopia. As for Ethiopian General Siyoum, although he was heard to be stationed in his birthplace of Achia Adti on Friday, his whereabouts are currently unknown. 20,000 Italian troops participated in this battle, with a total of 1,000 killed and wounded. The Ethiopian army killed more than 1,000 people. Chasing the defeated soldiers, which was previously the responsibility of the cavalry, is now carried out by aircraft, which is very effective. (Reuters, 1st) Italian Northern Front Headquarters: After General Badoglio defeated the troops of Ethiopian General Kassa in the northern part of the Tombien area, today the area is full of Ethiopian soldiers killed and wounded. Italian reconnaissance planes report that the Ethiopian Emperor's elite guard is now advancing north, hoping to make a final effort to stop the retreat of the defeated troops of General Kassa and General Siyoum. Today it is learned that the battle of Jinshan initially involved hand-to-hand combat in the dark. The Italian army advanced lightly and forced the Ethiopian army to abandon the defensive area on the top of the mountain. After hours of fierce fighting, the Italian army captured the Ethiopian army's general headquarters. Before retreating, the Ethiopian army also fought bravely. Now General Kassa's troops have retreated to the area where the rebellion is in full swing, and General Siyoum is hidden in a cave in the Tombien area, with only three or four soldiers left. (National Telegram, 1st)

Banknote Issuance Tax: Expected to No Longer Be Collected 44

Nanjing – The issue of collecting banknote issuance tax from various banks in the 15th year of the Republic of China is currently under consideration. Because the right of issuance of various banks was terminated when the legal tender was implemented, the reserve guarantee funds for those already issued and in circulation have been handed over to the Central Reserve Guarantee Fund Management Committee for safekeeping. The meaning of collecting the issuance tax was originally to prevent excessive issuance. Now that there is this restriction, it is expected that it will no longer be collected. It is still under study and has not yet been decided. (Special Dispatch, 2nd)

Nanjing – According to banking circles, in the past, in order to prevent banks from excessively issuing banknotes and to control the profits obtained by banks from issuing banknotes, the "Banknote Exchange Coupon Issuance Tax Law" was promulgated in the 20th year of the Republic of China, and the issuance tax was levied. Since the implementation of the new currency policy, the banknotes that each issuing bank had printed but not issued have now been sealed and destroyed. The cash and guarantee reserves that should be paid for the banknotes already issued and circulating in the market have also been taken over by the Issuance Reserve Management Committee. Now, except for the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, other banks no longer have the right of issuance, and naturally have no obligation to pay the issuance tax again. Even the banknotes issued by the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, which have the right of issuance, are now designated by the government as legal tender, and it seems that there is no reason to collect the issuance tax. The issuance tax for the 25th year of the Republic of China must be collected after the start of the fiscal year according to law. The date of collection is still far away. It is expected that the Ministry of Finance will have a clear expression on the issue of collecting the issuance tax around June 7th of this year. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

Silver Products: Ministry of Finance Approves That the "Silver Usage Management Rules" Need Not Be Amended 45

Nanjing – The national silversmith industry previously sent representatives to Nanjing to petition for the amendment of the "Silver Usage Management Rules for Silver Products" in order to maintain the livelihoods of silversmiths. The Ministry of Finance issued an approval on the 2nd, stating that the "Silver Usage Management Rules for Silver Products" promulgated by the Ministry are intended to control the use of silver, reduce the raw material costs of silver products, and promote the improvement of handicraft technology. In the implementation of the government's overall policy, it still maintains the intention of protecting the industry. As for the pure silver used in the rules, which must not exceed 30%, the Ministry has conducted detailed research and ordered the Central Mint to produce various alloy materials for use in handicraft technology, which will not hinder it. Still, it is necessary to follow the previous approved points and earnestly purchase and use them. (Central News Agency, 2nd)

Negotiations on the Hebei-Chahar Incident: Overview of Three Types of Taxes; Customs Duties Remain Normal, Salt Tax Reduced, Unified Tax Entirely Falls into Puppet Hands in Eastern Hebei 80

Tianjin Dispatch: Regarding the Hebei-Chahar incident, Doihara, representing the Japanese side, and Tada, the commander of the Japanese troops stationed in Tianjin, initially had divergent opinions and disagreements. After separate activities by Xiao Zhenying and Chen Zhongfu, they gradually moved toward consensus. Xiao Zhenying told people last week that he was very optimistic, saying that the puppet organization in eastern Hebei could be abolished within a week or so, with the only difference being the position of Yin Rugeng after he withdrew from eastern Hebei. Unexpectedly, the Tokyo coup broke out suddenly. Doihara, who belonged to the core of the young military faction, suddenly received a telegram to return home, and it is unlikely that he will come to Pingjin again in a short time. At the same time, Tada did not want to negotiate this matter before the political situation in his own country was settled, so the negotiations were shelved. At this time, the puppet organization in eastern Hebei is still proceeding with everything relentlessly, such as establishing a puppet construction committee, ordering each of the 22 counties in the puppet area to elect one representative to serve as a puppet committee member, and setting up a puppet propaganda agency in Tangshan City, the Eastern Hebei Daily, etc. Judging from the situation, there is no intention to abolish the puppet government. Therefore, there have been renewed rumors in recent days that problems have arisen regarding customs, salt, and unified taxes in the eastern Hebei region. According to inquiries from various parties, the rumors are exaggerated, and the facts have not yet changed significantly. As far as customs duties are concerned, the Tianjin Customs, Qinhuangdao Customs, and the various checkpoints on the Great Wall still collect taxes as before, and submit them to the Pingjin Central Bank in accordance with past procedures, which are then remitted to the Ministry of Finance. There are no obstacles to tax collection at various checkpoints. However, recently, according to the request of the North China authorities, the central government allocates 12 million yuan annually from customs revenue to assist with political expenses. The remaining amount, after deducting the 9 million yuan annually for customs surcharges, debt guarantees, etc., is approximately 20 million to 22 million yuan, which is returned to the central government. This general amount is based on last year's revenue as a distribution benchmark. The funds to assist the Hebei-Chahar authorities are directly allocated by the central government on a monthly basis. The tax revenue from various customs checkpoints has not been intercepted. As for salt taxes, the puppet government of eastern Hebei had previously sent puppet security teams to occupy the Tanggu and Hangu salt beaches, prohibiting the shipment of Changlu salt to other areas, and instead issuing new permits from the puppet finance office to transport Liaoning salt into the war zone for sale. After negotiations, it was resolved that 250,000 yuan would be allocated monthly for the puppet organization's political expenses, and more than 1.2 million yuan would be allocated for the military expenses of the Hebei-Chahar garrison. This matter was implemented in February. After the puppet government agreed, Changlu salt was allowed to be transported and sold as before. The puppet security team withdrew from the salt beaches. Changlu salt in the eastern Hebei region can also be sold. However, recently, the salt tax revenue has been low, with monthly revenue of less than 2 million yuan. After deducting various foreign debt guarantees and public debt repayments, the two assistance funds actually exceed 1.4 million yuan, which is already insufficient, so it is necessary to overdraw to supplement it. However, according to the tax bureau's observations, if the situation is stable, this year's tax revenue can still be maintained at the level of 20 million yuan last year, so there is no need to worry about deficits. As for the unified tax, after the Tangshan Unified Tax Administration was seized by the puppet government of eastern Hebei, the Ministry of Finance ordered the Tianjin Unified Tax Administration to also handle tax collection in other locations. For all goods from Tangshan and other eastern regions, when they pass through the first customs checkpoint on the sea route or the first unified tax inspection station on the land route, they are required to pay the tax. Tangshan's unified tax is mainly composed of coal tax from Kai'ao, cement tax from Qixin, cotton yarn tax from Huaxin Yarn Factory, and flour tax from Decheng Flour Factory, with a monthly revenue of more than 300,000 yuan. At first, the factory directors originally planned to pay taxes according to the old rules, but the puppet government's inspections were very strict. Those who did not pay taxes were not allowed to leave the factory for transport. The factory directors had no choice but to pay taxes according to the puppet regulations. When goods leave the eastern Hebei region, there are inspection stations on the land route and customs checkpoints on the sea route. If the tax is not paid, transport is not allowed. The factory directors believe that paying taxes twice is close to double taxation. Although they have protested, the political situation is such that empty talk and reasoning cannot be eliminated. Therefore, except for the coal tax from Linkuang, which is temporarily recorded on account and not paid to any party, the other factory directors negotiate with both parties. Those who transport and sell goods within the eastern Hebei region pay taxes to the puppet eastern Hebei government, and those who transport and sell goods outside the puppet area pay taxes to the Hebei-Chahar-Shanxi-Suiyuan unified tax agencies. The Japanese side had previously mediated between the two parties, intending to use a compromise method, using the total unified tax revenue of Hebei-Chahar as the standard, dividing it into four shares, with the puppet government of eastern Hebei taking one share and the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Council taking three shares. The North China authorities did not find this method very suitable and rejected it, so there is currently no way to reach a compromise. The Tanggu Unified Tax Administration Inspection Station, originally located in Tanggu, was ordered to move to Dagu to work because the area was occupied by the puppet eastern Hebei government. However, the unified tax revenue from Tangshan and other eastern regions is far lower than before, at most 30,000 to 40,000 yuan per month, a decrease of seven to eight times compared to the past. Due to the difficult environment, there is nothing to be done but sigh in vain. The unified tax of the four provinces of Hebei, Shanxi, Chahar, and Suiyuan, except for the revenue of Shanxi Province, which is retained for the province's public use, currently collects a total of more than 800,000 yuan in cash per month. The tax revenue from Tangshan has been withheld, and the current revenue is only more than 400,000 yuan. However, it has still been approved by the central government and allocated for Hebei-Chahar political expenses. (29th)

Juye County, Shandong Province: The Decayed Mouth of the Retaining Embankment is Blocked; Floodwater is Suddenly Blown Back by the Wind; County Magistrate Takes Advantage of the Situation to Supervise Construction; Disaster Victims in Five Counties Hope to Receive Relief 81

Jinan Dispatch: Since the Lingfan breach in Juye County, the repair of the Dong and Wang retaining embankments has failed one after another, and the floodwater has inundated almost the entire territory. On February 16, a strong northeast wind blew the floodwater into the Xinhe ditch, and the water level slowly dropped. By 6 p.m., the flow width at the mouth of the retaining embankment was only a few feet, and the water depth was only a foot or so. County Magistrate Qin Daoyu, upon receiving the report, believed that a good opportunity had arrived and immediately sent thousands of police and conscripted laborers to rush to block the breach overnight. The county magistrate also went to the breach in the wind at 10 p.m. to supervise the construction. However, although the water level had dropped, the ditch was quite deep, and the weather was cold and freezing, making it difficult to obtain soil. Moreover, the land before and after the retaining embankment was completely covered with accumulated water, so the work progressed with great difficulty. After ten days, the ditches were completely filled, and hemp bags and reeds were used to protect and consolidate them. A small embankment more than a hundred feet long and more than two feet wide was also built. The construction is still continuing. It is said that the decision has been made to make each new retaining embankment one zhang high and ten zhang thick. After it is completed, the breaches in the Dong and Wang retaining embankments will be repaired, and the work will be completed soon. The river defense will be further consolidated, and the million people in the five counties of Juye, Yuncheng, Fanxian, Shouyang, and Yanggu will all rejoice. It is said that the section of the Juye repaired embankment at the blockage point has the best results and was the first to be completed, which is very satisfactory. An order was also issued to the county to reward all personnel involved in the work. In addition to a major merit for the county magistrate, all other personnel involved in the work were also given merit and flags were awarded as encouragement. The Juye County Retaining Embankment, repaired by the people, was breached by accumulated ice on January 18, causing hundreds of villages in the five counties of Juye, Yuncheng, Fanxian, Shouyang, and Yanggu, north of Juye and south of Huanghua Temple, to be flooded. The disaster victims are suffering from hunger and cold and urgently need relief. Although the Yellow River Disaster Relief Association and the Relief Committee have allocated funds for emergency relief, it is a drop in the bucket and cannot solve the problem. Zhang Rugong, Xia Zhaogin, and five other representatives of the people from the five counties of Juye, Yuncheng, etc., were recently publicly recommended by the disaster victims to come to Jinan to appeal to the provincial government to quickly allocate funds for disaster relief, and to request the central government and various charitable organizations to urgently provide relief to save the people. Their petition states: "A petition regarding the breach of the people's embankment, the severity of the disaster, and the urgent need to allocate funds for relief to save the lives of the people. We have learned that the Juye Retaining Embankment, repaired by the people, was breached by the fierce rise of the river on January 18, causing hundreds of villages in the five counties of Juye, Yuncheng, Fanxian, Shouyang, and Yanggu, north of Juye and south of Huanghua Temple, to be flooded along the official embankment. The floodwaters are raging, and houses are collapsing. In this severe cold weather, with biting north winds, men, women, old, and young live in the open air, without enough clothing to keep warm and without enough food to fill their stomachs. They weep day and night, and deaths follow one another. The misery of the situation is unbearable to hear and unbearable to see. If relief is not provided, hundreds of thousands of people will surely starve to death. Your Honor is concerned about the people's suffering and loves the people like children. In past disasters, you have repeatedly provided relief, and the people are grateful for your virtue. Now we have suffered another great calamity, and relief is urgently needed. Therefore, we, the representatives, have crawled out of the mud and come here to appeal to the Chairman to show his grace again. The living and the dead will never forget it. We shed tears and submit this petition, humbly requesting your consideration. Presented to Chairman Han of the Shandong Provincial Government by Zhang Rugong, representative of Juye; Xia Zhaogin, representative of Yuncheng; Li Yantai, representative of Fanxian; Huang Zundian, representative of Shouzhang; and Lei Guangdian, representative of Yanggu." (29th)

Compilation of the Henan Gazetteer Completed: More Than Ten Million Words, Divided into 500 Volumes; Ancient Bronzes Form a Great Spectacle in the World 82

Kaifeng Dispatch: The Henan Gazetteer was started in the seventh year of the Republic of China and has taken eighteen years to compile, costing a total of more than 500,000 yuan. Now, all drafts have been completed, and proofreading can also be completed by the end of March. It is estimated that there are more than ten million words, which are planned to be divided into 500 volumes. The printing period will take at least half a year. The format is based on the Yuanhe Prefectural Gazetteer and the Yuanfeng Jiuyu Gazetteer, but a separate city and county gazetteer is added, describing the provincial capital, the traveling capital, the eleven special commissioner districts, and more than 110 counties, so that those who prepare the provincial gazetteer can avoid having to flip through the gazetteers of each county. The special features of the gazetteer, in addition to detailed descriptions of the province's soil, geology, animals, minerals, plants, clothing, food, and housing, are that the Jinshi Gazetteer is divided into two volumes. The upper volume contains those that have been recorded, and the lower volume of bronzes collects those preserved by the Anyang Antiquities Preservation Society, the Henan Museum, and the collectors Zhou Yang'an in Beiping, Liu Shanzhai in Shanghai, and Wu Yichang and Lin Shi'an in Henan, totaling more than 500 pieces. According to world-renowned works on Chinese ancient bronzes, the most famous are Yunshi's Jijinglu and the Essence of Chinese Ancient Bronzes in Japan, but the former has less than 200 pieces and the latter has less than 300 pieces. This gazetteer will become a great spectacle in the world. Regarding dialects, it first describes the position of the Henan dialect in the Chinese dialect system and its origin, the mixing of ancient Hua and Hu, the reclamation of Hukuang in the Ming Dynasty, and its relationship with the Henan dialect. It then describes the characteristics of the tones and final sounds, dividing the province into ten linguistic regions, including Kaifeng, Shangqiu, Anyang, Linzhang, Wuzhi, Qinyang, Runan, Xinyang, Luoyang, and Shanxian. The compilers of the gazetteer include Chief Editor Hu Shiqing, former source stream Zhang Guogan, official Wu Tingxie, literature Xie Guozhen, Jinshi Liu Jie, household population clan surname Li Taifen, religion Liu Pansui, and others such as Wang Youqiao, Zhang Zhongfu, Jiang Huiwu, etc., all of whom are specialists in their fields. (February 29th)

Fujian Province Establishes Provincial Land Bureau to Manage Land Throughout the Province 83

Fuzhou Dispatch: The provincial government has recently established the Provincial Land Bureau to reorganize land throughout the province, appointing Gao Dengting as the director and He Jingwei as the deputy director. Yao Yonghuang, Fan Hongzhen, Shi Lin, etc. are appointed as section chiefs, He Youzao as accounting director, and Zhao Ju'en as technical director. The remaining staff are filled by original staff from the Land Administration Section of the Department of Civil Affairs and graduates from the Finance Class of the County Administration Personnel Training Institute. It was established on March 1. As for the land reports from various counties, after the provincial government urged them to speed up the process, two-thirds have now been completed. The remaining one-third of the counties have not been completed, either due to financial difficulties or lack of talent, resulting in slow progress. After the establishment of the Land Bureau, it was decided that all counties must complete the process by the end of June this year. Those counties that have already completed the process will continue to conduct land surveying. The provincial government has already telegraphed Minhou and Changle counties to quickly plan and conduct a complete land survey of the county, and to submit the preparation situation and budget for expenses so that personnel can be sent to provide guidance. After receiving the order, the Minhou County Government has appointed Gan Jiaen to be responsible for the planning. It is expected that the surveying can begin in mid-April. The method is to first organize ten small surveying teams, select a certain area, and implement the land registration according to the township, step by step. After the efficiency of the team improves, it will be expanded to sixty small teams, and then a general survey and registration will be carried out. The estimated total cost is 200,000 yuan. The Minhou County Government stated that it will not collect surveying donations from the people for this surveying expense, but those who hide or underreport their land will be punished. (February 29th)

Lianghuai Salt Transport Agency Maintains Wharf and Bengbu Salt Sales, Clearly Stating That Salt From Other Areas is Not Allowed to Encroach on Sales 84

Bengbu Dispatch: Bengbu is a wharf for the sale of Huai salt. All incoming salt must be put into warehouses and sold in turn, which is the so-called rotation system. As time goes by, the costs increase. The salt from Mingguang and Guzhen arrives and is sold immediately, with lower costs. Therefore, it is difficult for the Bengbu salt price to be on par with Mingguang and Guzhen. Last year, a small number of merchants transported salt from Mingguang and Guzhen to sell in Bengbu and the Hebei area, which greatly affected the sale of rotated salt. In order to maintain the Huai salt rotation sales system, the Lianghuai Salt Transport Agency recently telegraphed the Bengbu Salt Affairs Tax Collection Office and Inspection Bureau, ordering that no matter what method of transportation is used, the salt from Guzhen is not allowed to be sold to the south, and the salt from Mingguang is not allowed to be sold to the north. The tax police of the office are responsible for strictly enforcing this. If any salt that violates the regulations is found, it should be deposited in Bengbu and listed after the existing old salt, to be sold in turn, so as to avoid taking advantage of loopholes. All salt that has been taxed but not transported is not allowed to change the designated transport location. After receiving the order, the Tax Collection Office here, in addition to sending letters to the Jiashan and Guzhen Inspection Offices to sell the salt stored in their respective locations and not to issue Northern and Southern transport inspection certificates to encroach on Bengbu sales, also sent letters to the military and police agencies to assist the office's tax police in strictly cracking down on violations in order to maintain rotation sales. (29th)

Songjiang 85

The Xinzhuang Gambling Case is Referred to the Court

The Public Security Bureau, on February 24, received a secret report that there were large gambling tables in the Huizhenguan Taoist Temple in Xinzhuang Town, with all kinds of gambling activities, such as Yaoshi 20-Door Pai Gow, and hundreds of gamblers gathered. Outside, Shen opera was performed, ostensibly to raise funds, with tickets priced at one yuan and eight jiao, ostensibly to attract spectators, but in reality to attract gamblers. The bureau sent patrol officers, squad leaders, detectives, and a plainclothes police officer to make arrests. They saw members of the Security Corps guarding the entrance. They arrested four gamblers inside, including Wang Yongfa, Zhu Fangsheng, Chen Yongjin, and Wang Yongsheng, as well as gambling equipment such as the 20-Door Guan Tan Pu. They were detained at the 6th Precinct. Patrol Officer Lu, believing that the ringleader had not been caught, temporarily released the detainees on bail. Director He then sent a superintendent to investigate and confirmed the report. However, the gambling ringleader could not be found. After reporting back to the bureau, he telegraphed Patrol Officer Lu to transfer the detainees and evidence to Songjiang. However, Wang Yongsheng had already fled. The bureau then transferred Wang's guarantor, Guan Jichang, along with the other three detainees and gambling evidence, to Songjiang yesterday. After Director He personally interrogated them, except for the guarantor Guan Jichang, who was ordered to find Wang Bingsheng and send him to the authorities, the remaining detainees were sent to the County Court for interrogation.

Suzhou 86

Yue City Discovered Outside Xumen Gate

Jiang Dayi, an archaeologist from Suzhou, discovered an ancient city on November 24 last year in Wangbi, 24th Ward, outside the Xumen Gate of this county. According to the local gazetteer, this is the Yue City built by the King of Yue when he attacked Wu. Zhang Feng and other archaeologists from Shanghai also came to investigate after hearing the news. On the 29th, Wei Juxian came to Suzhou to give a lecture and also saw the city. Wei, who had initiated the Wu-Yue History and Geography Research Association with Wu Zhihui and Ye Yuhu, also recognized that the city was of great importance to the historical sites of Wu and Yue.

Farmers From Chefang Town Swarm Into the City

One day, six to seven hundred farmers suddenly came from Chefang Town, Suzhou, and swarmed into the street. All the shops closed their doors. The 6th Precinct of the Public Security Bureau received a report and armed itself to cut off the streets, alleys, and bridges. At the same time, it invited Song and Dong, local figures, and the Baojia chiefs to persuade the farmers not to disrupt the order. At the same time, the 2nd Squad of the 3rd Company of the 7th Security Brigade stationed in Chefang also came out to defend the Hexi area. At that time, the farmers were quite noisy. Patrol Officer Zhou persuaded them that those who owed rent should pay the rent, and that requests for reductions should be discussed at length. The farmers' representatives were satisfied. By 3 p.m., they began to leave the town in a steady stream. The defense of Chefang was not relaxed until the evening.

Wuxi 87

The Commissioner's Office is Established in One Day

Zang Qifang, the Administrative Inspector of the Wuxi District, arrived in the town the day before yesterday after being appointed. He paid visits to the heads of the provincial departments and offices to ask for instructions. Then, on the evening of the day before yesterday, he arrived in Wuxi with personnel from various departments. At 10 a.m. one day, he established the Commissioner's Office at the Donation and Tax Collection Office on Gongyuan Road and immediately began his duties. He has appointed Hong Sheng as the secretary, Liu Shaoyan as the head of the First Section, Cui De as the head of the Second Section, and Bai Zhujun, the original training officer of the Wuxi District Security Team, as the secretary-general of the Security Command. Wu Delin is the chief of staff. The majority of other administrative personnel have also been appointed. The Wuxi Court is Promoted to a First-Class Court

The Wuxi Local Sub-Court was established in January 1931. After three years, it was changed back to the County Court, handling primary appeal cases from the four counties of Xi, Cheng, Yi, and Piao. Later, with the reform of the judicial system to a three-level, three-trial system, it was changed back to the District Court, expanding the scope of private prosecution. Last month, Wang Yongbin, Minister of Justice, went to various counties along the Beijing-Shanghai line to inspect the judiciary. Because Wuxi is located in an important area, with a mixed population of locals and migrants, and civil and criminal lawsuits are increasing daily, it cannot be compared with other counties. It was decided that at the beginning of this year, it would be promoted to a first-class court at the same time as the Jiangdu District Court, and a prosecutor would be added. It has been internally decided to transfer the current Judge Lu to fill the position, and Prosecutor Shen Zhaoming will be promoted to a regular prosecutor. A chief prosecutor will still be established, with the current Judge Cheng Jun filling the position. Additional judges and clerks will also be appointed to the trial section. In the future, its powers and position will be completely equal to those of the Wuxian District Court.

The Hexutai Gambling Den is Cracked

The Hexutai in Tanhang, outside the North Gate, was originally a famous gambling den. It was taken over by Dai Alin this year, renamed the Xinsheng Tea Garden, and continued to operate as a gambling den every day, with extremely large sums of money involved. The day before yesterday evening, Wang Ji, the superintendent of the County Public Security Bureau, secretly sent many patrol officers to search the premises. Ninety-five male and female gamblers and various gambling tools were arrested. After being taken to the bureau, they were all transferred to the court for interrogation on the morning of the one day.

The Tricycle Pullers' Union is Established

The tricycle pullers of Wujin County had previously experienced a labor strike due to the problem of vehicle rental. The strike was resolved after mediation by Party and government agencies. The tricycle pullers, feeling the lack of a legitimate organization, began preparing to organize a union in the autumn of last year.
