Finance: Indian Silver Plummets; Speculation on Gold; But Result Still a Drop of Eight Cents 189

Yesterday, the gold market remained uncertain and unstable. The market trended downwards due to weakening confidence, but showed some support after the initial drop. Ultimately, the price of Indian silver plummeted, triggering a surge in buying interest. At the start of the morning session, overseas silver markets in the UK and US were stable, with no activity on the ground. Forward silver prices in Montreux fluctuated, exchange rates remained unchanged, and the price of raw gold in London rose by one penny. The official exchange rates announced by the Central Bank remained unchanged for both the UK and US, and the Customs Gold Unit remained unchanged. The official standard gold price was raised to 1,147.90 yuan, but confidence seemed to weaken. Off-market forward trades opened at around 49.50 yuan, and major firms such as Dadecheng, Shunmao, Dafa, and Yongyuanmao sold off, pushing the price down to around 8 yuan. The morning opening was low but remained stable. However, major firms were keen to sell, leading to oversupply and a temporary drop. Sellers then took a wait-and-see approach, and support gradually emerged at the lower prices, stabilizing the overall trend. The HSBC exchange rates for the UK and US remained unchanged, as did the silver balance tax, resulting in a quiet and uneventful market. Later, buying interest increased, gradually driving prices up. The market trend remained stable at midday, but the announcement of a ten-anna drop in the price of Indian silver in the afternoon triggered a buying frenzy, pushing prices up. Despite some resistance after the second announcement of stable Indian silver prices, rumors persisted, buying interest remained strong, and the price rose to 1,150 yuan. Major firms sold off at the higher prices, and the final trend stabilized again. The day's market conditions are recorded below.

The morning opening was 1,148.20 yuan, a drop of 1.70 yuan from last Saturday. Fuxingyong and Huixiang made gains to 8.60 yuan. Dadecheng, Dafa, Yongchunyuan, and Yong sold off, pushing the price down to 7.70 yuan. The Central Bank offered US dollars at 25. Dadecheng and Dingkang made gains to 8.40 yuan. Dadecheng, Dafa, Yonghuixiang, Shunmao, Shenda, and Yong sold off, dropping to 7 yuan. Tianfa and Qianyuan made gains to 7.60 yuan. Huixiang and Dafa sold off to 7.30 yuan. Fuxingyong and Huixiang took advantage of the lower prices to make gains to 7.70 yuan. The HSBC exchange rates remained unchanged. Richang, Chunyuan, Yong, Fuxingyong sold off to 7.30 yuan again. Futaiyong and Dadecheng entered the market. The silver balance tax remained unchanged, rising to 7.80 yuan. Dafayong and Zhichang sold off to 7.50 yuan. Futaiyong, Qingfayong, Yongyuanmao, Yonghuixiang, Qiafengyong, and Qianchangxiang jointly purchased orders, gradually rising to 8.60 yuan. Fuxingyong and Dadecheng sold off at the higher prices to 7.90 yuan. Qingfayong, Richang, and Dingkang purchased orders, gradually rising to 8.70 yuan. The midday closing was 1,148.50 yuan.

The afternoon opening was 1,148.50 yuan. Chunyuan, Hengyu, Qiafengyong, Dafayong, and Richang sold off, dropping to 8 yuan. Jinfengyong, Qingfayong, Dingkang, Richang, Fuxingyong, Lifeng, Futaiheng, Chunyuan, Wanxing, Renfayong, Yuanyi, and Huixiang competed to enter the market. Shen Bao Medical and Pharmaceutical Supplement

Overview of the Work in the Jiangsu Provincial Zhenjiang Rural Health Experiment Zone (Part 2) 210

— Zhu Yunda

Work Overview

A. Healthcare Work: Environmental hygiene, street cleaning, adopt household self-management. Each household is responsible for the garbage in front of its own door and maintains cleanliness. This method can cultivate a sense of automatic cleanliness and hygiene habits among rural residents and must be strictly supervised and encouraged to be effective. Over the past few months, the streets have gradually become cleaner, ash piles have been gradually removed, and garbage is no longer discarded randomly as in the past. It is very difficult to eliminate open-air manure vats in rural areas, because manure is a useful item in the countryside, and every household has one or two vats for storing manure. We can only teach them to move or destroy those that are detrimental to public and family hygiene. We cover the ones allowed to exist with straw mats made of rice straw. This method does not cost money and can be done by rural households. At the same time, these vats are numbered with lime water on the outside of the vat, to prevent further increase. At the end of last year, we registered and numbered 494 of them in Jianbi alone. There are 37 toilets in the entire town. We prescribed two designs for them to be improved. One is fly-proof and the other is odor-removing. The former is equipped with a spring-loaded active door, screens and lighting windows, and a cover on the manure collection point. Each improvement like this costs about ten yuan, which rural people already find burdensome. Therefore, fifteen places adopted the fly-proof modification, and the rest of the households adopted the odor-removing method. The latter method costs only two or three yuan per toilet, which is bearable for households with financial difficulties. Along the riverbank, people are prohibited from dumping sewage and pollutants in places where drinking water is taken. People already know that polluted drinking water is harmful to everyone’s health. They persuade and supervise each other. Recently, dirty things are no longer dumped into the river, and dirty things are no longer washed in the river. At the same time, it is stipulated that tea houses and shops must have two tanks, one for use and one for alum-purified water for standby, and both must be covered. Teacups and towels must be soaked in boiling water every day. Sanitation-related industries, such as teahouses, wine shops, barbershops, bathhouses, etc., have been registered and managed, and various sanitary equipment has been added. People already feel the urgent need to rectify the blocked ditches. Local people are now initiating fundraising for repairs. The technical aspects are jointly undertaken by this office and the Zhenjiang County Government. This matter is progressing actively and is scheduled to begin repairs in mid-March or April of this year. School Hygiene: There are four county-run elementary schools in the district: Jianbi Elementary School, Xie Gou Elementary School, Qian Wei Elementary School, and Liang Shan Elementary School, with a total of more than 350 students. When we first arrived, in order to understand the physical health of children in rural areas, we conducted a physical examination of children in the district, examining a total of 22 elementary schools and private schools, checking 724 people. Those with defects accounted for 64.2% of the total number. Trachoma, malnutrition, and skin diseases were the most common. The classification of defects was: trachoma 24.2%, nutrition 31%, skin 23%, vision 16%, teeth 13%, hearing 8.6%, tonsils 3.4%, others 1.4% (Many people have several defects). After the examination, we treated patients with trachoma, skin diseases, and tonsil diseases. For those who are malnourished, we instruct them on the combination of plant foods and methods of obtaining nutrients. After this examination, we felt that it was necessary to organize school hygiene. We first conducted a children's health education experiment at Jianbi Elementary School, adopting a student guidance system. Twenty-four outstanding students were selected from each grade to form a health team, divided into four groups: health care, epidemic prevention, medical affairs, and publicity. Doctors and nurses from this office take turns training them at the school. After the training period, the health team members will teach other students, using the children’s close experience, close attitude and language to teach children and implement children teaching children, children leading children. The educational method is that the members of the health team cannot but set an example by themselves and pay attention to their own cleanliness because they have to teach other students. We will also review the students’ hygiene knowledge and behavior, as well as the work of the health team members from time to time, evaluate and improve students’ love of cleanliness and autonomy. Staff are often sent to guide other elementary schools and private schools and hold health talks. It is now planned that after the start of the spring semester this year, schools such as Qianwei, Xiegou, and Liangshan will also start the same health team training. Maternal and Infant Hygiene: Rural women give birth at the whim of old-fashioned midwives or family members. Childbirth often turns into death. At the beginning of the establishment of this office, we launched a free delivery service and paid attention to prenatal check-ups. Everyone who came for consultation was told about physiological knowledge, such as the size of the fetal position and pelvis, the distance of the delivery date, and all precautions that pregnant women should take. After delivery, the puerperal women also underwent multiple examinations and visits. Although it has only been open for a few months, as a result of our publicity and the introduction of Mothers’ Association members, many people believe in the new method of delivery. Midwives Wu Ruoshui and Jin Peiyu have a spirit of hard work. When it snows at night and the rural roads are bad, even small cars cannot be used, so they have to walk. The longest round trip takes seven or eight miles, but they are very happy and don’t feel any hardship. The next day, the villagers wrapped a few red eggs or vegetables and sent them to us, thanking us repeatedly. The honest and loyal attitude of the villagers is commendable. Midwife Training Class: In order to reduce the midwives’ resentment and arouse their belief in new methods of delivery, a midwife training class was held. The first phase of training included a total of six midwives from Jianbi Town. The courses included: 1. Outline of obstetrical physiology and anatomy, 2. Outline of bacteria, 3. Introduction to sterilization and methods, 4. Common sense of pregnancy and puerperal pathology, 5. Umbilical cord handling method, 6. Pre-delivery equipment and procedures, 7. Outline of prenatal and postnatal care, 8. Infant care method, 9. Usage of obstetrical tools and medicines, 10. Method of resuscitation of pseudo-dead newborns, 11. Puerperal woman care method, 12. Internship. The training period is set for 14 days, with two hours of lectures per day. After the training period, in addition to issuing midwife qualification certificates, each person will be given a set of disinfection basins, cotton gauze, and disinfection medicines. 5. Infant Health Experiment Station: There is a Infant Receiving Bureau in Jianbi, with a total of 128 infants fostered outside. The maximum number of infants kept inside is eight, and the minimum is two or three. Those fostered outside are subsidized by the Bureau for 5,000 copper coins per month to the foster mother, which are collected on a monthly basis. Subsidies stop after the infant turns six years old, and the child belongs to the foster mother. It costs five or six yuan per month to hire a wet nurse to feed a baby, which is more expensive. Therefore, the Bureau holds the purpose of "sending it out immediately". Therefore, there are very few infants in the inner hall. There are three reasons why children are abandoned in rural areas: 1. They are unable to support them, 2. The baby is sick and difficult to cure, 3. Illegitimate children. The former two are the most common reasons. Since the background of the infants sent is like this, the environment of the foster family is even more unmentionable. The foster mothers who come to the Infant Receiving Bureau to pick up babies are all poor farmers who cannot afford a cone. Taking advantage of their own fertility and lactation, they take another child to earn 5,000 copper coins per month for living expenses (some are because their own baby has died). Under these circumstances, the fate of abandoned children, even if they reach the Infant Receiving Bureau for relief, cannot escape the tragic pain of early death.

The Impact of Food on Infant Eczema 211

— Xie Yunshou

Infant eczema often occurs on the head and face, sometimes spreading to the entire body. Oozing fluids and layered scabs cause infants to scratch day and night, leading to restlessness, sleeplessness, gradual emaciation, and poor nutrition. Furthermore, this type of eczema is often difficult to cure quickly, sometimes lasting for months or even years. Although there is no definitive theory regarding the cause of eczema, food has a definite relationship to it. This can be stated definitively based on clinical experience. The following is an explanation of how food affects infant eczema.

The idea that food is a cause of infant eczema originated with American medical doctor Blackfan in 1916. He believed that food has a significant relationship to the occurrence of eczema in infants. In the last decade, a portion of European scholars have also acknowledged this view. His experimental method involved making multiple small cuts on the apparently healthy skin of infants suffering from eczema, then applying various food-derived proteins. Alternatively, diluted solutions of these proteins were injected intradermally in small amounts to observe any reactions at the application or injection site. The results showed that in infants with eczema, the application site quickly developed noticeable redness and slight swelling. When the same was done on healthy infants or infants without eczema, this reaction did not occur. From this, it was concluded that these proteins must have some causal relationship to the development of eczema. If eczema is caused by these proteins, then removing them should lead to a cure. However, among proteins, egg white, cow's milk, and breast milk are the most likely to cause eczema. While completely removing them may benefit the eczema, it can also hinder the infant's nutrition.

The phenomenon where a certain protein can cause eczema is medically referred to as "Allergen." The eczema and other phenomena caused by this "Allergen" are medically termed "Allergie." "Allergie" essentially carries the meaning of hypersensitivity and idiosyncrasy. So, how does this food-derived "Allergen" act? It can be divided into two types: congenital, acquired through the placenta, and acquired, passed through breast milk. When such conditions exist, the infant, from its food, such as breast milk or artificial formula, encounters the foreign protein and experiences the phenomenon of "Allergie," resulting in eczema. However, sometimes eczema doesn't occur, and instead, urticaria (hives) or asthma may develop. This has not yet been fully explained.

The occurrence of eczema results from idiosyncrasy and hypersensitivity, the so-called "Allergie" state. But why is this "Allergie" limited to certain infants and not all infants? In the acquired theory, the following inducing factors are necessary, for example:

1. Systemic infectious diseases as inducing factors. For example, after measles or vaccination, becoming "Allergie," resulting in adenopathic eczema, etc., is commonly experienced by us.

2. Local sensitization inducing "Allergie." For example, after developing febrile airway inflammation, influenza, or bronchitis, adenopathic eczema, urticaria, eczema, etc., often occur.

3. When there is an impairment in the digestive and absorptive functions of the gastrointestinal tract. For example, abnormal digestive fluid secretion, inflammation of the gastrointestinal tract, and other diseases, or drinking alcoholic beverages, coffee, and other stimulating foods that damage the walls of the digestive tract, proteins that have not been fully digested and broken down pass through the digestive tract walls into the bloodstream, causing eczema.

4. When the detoxification function of the liver is weakened due to some reason.

5. Changes occur in the distribution of bacteria in certain parts of the gastrointestinal tract. Decomposed food components, through the action of bacteria, produce abnormal toxic decomposition products, promoting the absorption of "Allergen."

6. Endocrine disorders. For example, when there are disorders of the thyroid or ovaries.

7. In addition, the stimulation of the skin by light, heat, cold, chemical substances, and changes in food.

In summary, when the above-mentioned various impairments exist as precursors, the state of "Allergie" is easily provoked by certain food components, leading to the occurrence of eczema. The above is for the acquired type. As for the congenital type, "Allergie" is obtained from the placenta. A certain protein passes through the damaged or inflamed digestive tract of the mother, enters the bloodstream, and reaches the infant's body, or the mother consumes too much of the same food.

Among animal-derived proteins, egg white and cow's milk are the most likely to cause infant eczema. Among plant-derived proteins, wheat flour is the most likely. In addition, there are egg yolk, wheat paste, potatoes, carrots, bananas, buckwheat, etc. Besides protein, there are butter, sucrose, etc. The following describes the major ones:

A. Chicken Eggs: Among animal-derived proteins, chicken eggs are the most significant, especially egg white. Therefore, some people advocate that egg white allergy is the cause of infant eczema. The reason why egg white becomes an allergen is said to be due to the albumin in egg white, mucin, and mucoid. Egg yolk is far less significant than egg white and thus not worthy of attention. Infants born to mothers who overeat chicken eggs or infants nourished with chicken eggs are prone to eczema. Or if the mother continues to consume chicken eggs, the eczema is difficult to cure or even worsens. Conversely, if chicken eggs are removed from the mother's diet, the infant's eczema lightens or is even cured. Raw chicken eggs are more problematic than cooked chicken eggs.

B. Cow's Milk: Although less severe than chicken eggs, it is also an important factor. Therefore, when eczema occurs in infants nourished with cow's milk, and a causal relationship is suspected, cow's milk must be eliminated. However, prohibiting milk for infants who rely on cow's milk for nutrition is a major issue. If unavoidable, employing a wet nurse or switching to goat's milk, prolonged boiling of cow's milk, or milk-free foods can lighten or cure the eczema.

C. Human Milk: Some people claim that it is related, but it is mostly insignificant.

D. Bird and Animal Meat: These are mostly not directly ingested by the infant but rather come from breast milk after the mother consumes them. The relationship is very small.

E. Plant-Derived Proteins: Wheat flour is the most significant. According to a report by Ratanel, a seven-and-a-half-month-old infant developed intensely itchy dry eczema on both cheeks. Inquiring about the mother's condition during pregnancy revealed that she had consumed foods made with wheat flour extensively. There was also an infant who, for six months, was exclusively breastfed and later developed eczema after being given bread. Therefore, experiments by various researchers have shown that wheat is the most significant among plant-derived proteins. Rice can be used as a substitute at this time. In addition, potatoes, oats, rye, barley, rice, corn, carrots, bananas, apples, grapes, etc., are all related to infant eczema.

F. Fats: This relationship is not very significant. Some believe that butter can cause eczema, and others think that chocolate is related.

G. Carbohydrates: This relationship is also minimal. Some claim that sucrose is related. For example, when sucrose is added to the cow's milk of a certain infant, the eczema worsens. Removing it leads to a cure. Giving brewer's yeast is said to cure it.

Although there has been clear experimentation on the relationship between the above-mentioned foods and eczema, there are also many opponents. These are briefly omitted.

On the Construction of Medicine and Pharmaceuticals with Chinese Subjectivity (Part 2) 212

— Song Guobin

Old Medicine Scientized; New Medicine Sinicized

Second: The nationalization of medical education. It is well known that the introduction of modern medicine into China began with the missionaries from the West coming to China, so although it has been a long time, the hospitals and art schools established by the churches still exist in the country. When the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, there was a plan to reclaim educational rights, and the voices at that time were loud and clear, with a strong momentum for improvement. However, looking at it now, what is the result? The greatest purpose of foreign-established schools is to train service personnel for their businesses in China to facilitate their cultural aggression. The smallest trick is to eliminate students' national concepts through anesthesia methods, making them forget that they are Chinese youth. The so-called subjectivity is completely based on them, not on us. Therefore, the courses listed, the textbooks adopted, the language spoken, and the writing used are all based on their country. How can one expect students to know how to take China as the subject in such a situation? Is it not like going south while heading north? Therefore, if educational rights are not reclaimed for one day, the construction of modern medicine with Chinese subjectivity cannot be realized for one day. This is the second point. (Note: The so-called reclaiming of educational rights refers to the fact that the administrative power of a school cannot be controlled by foreigners, while the hiring of foreign scholars as professors is not included in this example.)

Third: The nationalization of medical administration. A country has its own sovereignty, and a country that is not a colony has independent sovereignty. Although the health administration of our country is directly under the jurisdiction of the central government, it is actually in the hands of a certain foreign trust. There may be unavoidable difficulties in this, and it may not be possible to get rid of it for a while. However, being controlled by others is often restrictive, and it is ultimately impossible to seek free development and independent construction. Therefore, reclaiming the power of health administration is an urgent task at present. Without this, the construction based on China as the subject will inevitably be full of thorns. This is the third point.

Fourth: The nationalization of the medical profession. Confucius said: "Only fame and tools cannot be lent to others." Lending fame leads to abuse, and lending tools damages oneself.

Regardless of whether a country is strong or weak, the people have their rights to enjoy and the responsibility to protect, which the government bears. If the rights that the people of this country should enjoy are given to foreign residents, what is the difference between cutting off one's own flesh to give to others? The medical profession is of utmost importance, relating to the strength or weakness of the race and the lives of the people! Therefore, all countries in Europe and the West spare no effort to protect medical rights. All foreign doctors are restricted from practicing in their own country, because they are not of our race, so they have no sympathy. They do not understand the national conditions, which on the one hand endangers the lives of the people, and on the other hand damages the rights and interests of domestic doctors. How can the lives and rights of the people be used as exchange products for diplomacy at no cost! Because of its weakness, our country is limited by unequal treaties, allowing foreign doctors to come to China to practice, which has led to the loss of rights and interests and the endangerment of people's lives. Thinking of this, it is truly heartbreaking! I have often thought that the reason why countries in Europe and the West restrict foreign doctors is that they attach importance to the concept of basing everything on the nation and the people's occupation. The national and national concepts of our people seem to be lighter than those of Western Europe, and they have always advocated the open-door policy, which has led to the position of the new medical community today. Isn't this the biggest obstacle to its localization? Therefore, it is necessary to urge the government to formulate and implement regulations for the management of foreign doctors practicing in China as soon as possible! This is the fourth point.

The above four points are all about medicine. Please speak again about the nationalization of new drugs: First, the management of foreign drugs. In recent years, imported drugs have accounted for a large proportion of imports, and the annual leakage is truly an alarming figure. If we conduct an assessment, we will find that they are uneven in quality, some are effective, some are ineffective, some are outdated, and some are harmful. All of them are allowed to be sold in China, which is related to the lives of the people, and it is not just a matter of foreign rights and interests! In the past, the medical community in our country had a move to identify proprietary medicines, but recently it has tended to decline! I sincerely hope that the government will clearly stipulate regulations for the management of foreign drugs, and that the medical community will jointly bear the responsibility of inspecting foreign drugs, in order to protect the safety of the people's lives and recover the rights and interests to the greatest extent possible, because we regard the people's lives and rights as the subject of the country. This is the first point. Second, the imitation of raw materials. The above-mentioned methods for managing foreign drugs are still passive precautions and are not sufficient to be called active resistance. They are still policies of dependence and are not sufficient to be called independent construction. How can we actively resist? Do not use imported goods. How can we build independently? Imitate the raw materials of Western medicines. Therefore, the management of foreign drugs only eliminates the obstacles to subjectivity, while the imitation of raw materials is the first step in the construction of subjectivity. This is the second point. Third, the creation of domestic new drugs. The effectiveness of domestic medicines has long been known to the world, but unfortunately, we are unwilling to place them, so that these valuable raw materials are buried in barren beaches and poor valleys. If we can study them one by one with scientific methods, we can create some effective and good medicines, which can greatly compete for a place in international pharmaceutical science, not just resist imported goods! This is the third point. The above is all about medicine, so what I call the construction of Chinese medicine and medicine with Chinese subjectivity is different from empty talk!

In summary, there are passive resistance and active construction! The two complement each other and serve each other. Therefore, if the invasion of imported medicine and medicine is not eliminated, there is no hope for the development of Chinese new medicine and medicine: If medical education and medical administration cannot be completely independent, how can we plan the construction of Chinese medicine and medicine with Chinese subjectivity? I have often thought that the civilization of Europe today originated from Greece and Rome, but its brilliance is a hundred or a thousand times greater than that of Greece and Rome at that time. Why? Because it can absorb the essence of Greek and Roman culture without submerging its own personality? China, from the Han Dynasty to the Song Dynasty, was the most prosperous period of culture. At that time, Indian Buddhism was introduced into China, and Chinese scholars took its essence and integrated it with the inherent philosophy of Laozi and Confucius, thus creating an independent Chinese philosophy. Although India has perished to this day, China should take the first seat in the world's Buddhist studies. From this, it can be seen that the Chinese nation has the ability to absorb and assimilate foreign civilizations! Today's acceptance of Western science is like accepting Indian civilization in those days. The key lies in getting its spirit and using its methods, but not swallowing it whole, not asking whether it is suitable for our taste, and stuffing it into our stomachs in a muddle-headed way. It is rare for those who do not develop gastrointestinal diseases! If we understand this, we can talk about the construction of Chinese medicine and medicine with Chinese subjectivity.

Common Discussion of Measles 213

— Qu Yahong

Measles is commonly known as "shazi" (痧子). This disease is almost a necessary infectious disease for children. As the saying goes, everyone is bound to get "shazi." If you don't get it while alive, you'll have to get it after death. Such absurd talk is, of course, not worth believing. However, the fact that children are very susceptible to infection proves that society has a deep understanding of it. However, because there has been a lack of research into its causes and treatments, many young lives continue to be sacrificed. Now is the time of spring, and this disease is spreading like bamboo shoots after the rain. I am now going to talk about the origins and course of this disease, hoping that readers will pay attention.

Cause: Although the causative agent of this disease is not yet fully understood, it has been determined that it is an infectious disease.

Symptoms: The initial symptoms of this disease are exactly like a common cold. It's just coughing, runny nose, fever, decreased appetite, and general unhappiness. People often don't pay much attention. By the time the eyes are red, light-sensitive, teary, the fever is high and persistent, and the person is listless, seeing red spots is when they realize it's measles, but it's already too late. In fact, in the early stages, if you carefully examine the inner cheek area opposite the canines and molars, you can definitely find small white spots the size of sesame seeds. The white spots are surrounded by a reddish halo. Because these are born inside the skin and flesh, unlike milk spots, they cannot be easily wiped away. We call them Koplik's spots. These spots are a unique precursor to measles, so seeing these spots allows you to confirm measles early. After two or three days, red rashes about the size of mung beans first appear on the face, and then spread relatively quickly to the whole body. The temperature also rises with it to around 39-40 degrees Celsius. After one or two days, the red rash gradually subsides and the temperature gradually decreases. At the same time, dandruff-like skin flakes fall off. If the condition is mild and well-treated, the patient will recover within this short period. If, after four or five days, the fever does not subside, or the rash suddenly disappears midway, these are signs of other complications. We must pay attention to the examination. The most common complications are pneumonia, otitis media, diphtheria, and cancrum oris (俗名走馬疳). In this way, how can that weak and delicate patient withstand the torment of disease on top of disease? Naturally, there is a danger to life.

Treatment: Currently, the only effective medical treatments for measles are the blood serum of patients who have had measles and are in the recovery phase, and the blood serum of the patient's biological mother. There are no other particularly effective medicines. However, general symptomatic treatment is also essential. There is one thing that I especially hope that patients' families will pay great attention to, which is that the indoor temperature should always be maintained at around 18-20 degrees Celsius. Although it is said that you cannot be exposed to drafts, the indoor air should always be well-circulated. The temperature should also not be too dry. In my experience, during the period when the patient is incubating the disease and does not yet know whether it is a rash or not, the patient's family, due to economic or other reasons, brings the patient to the doctor's house for diagnosis and treatment. On the way to and from, they unknowingly add wind-cold, so that the light ones become heavy and the heavy ones become fatal. The patient's family may mistakenly blame the ineffectiveness of the medicine. Isn't this a wrong to both sides? Therefore, all patients with measles, especially young infants, must be sent to the hospital as soon as possible. This is not only convenient for treatment, but also avoids the trouble of going back and forth, and can prevent the transmission of the disease to other children in the home. For families who cannot or do not want to send the patient to the hospital, the doctor must be invited to the home. Other children should also be completely isolated from the patient.

Hygiene Knowledge of Ear, Nose, Throat and Eye Diseases 214

— Tang Renjin

(79) The Relationship Between Syphilis and Nasal Diseases (Continued)

Tertiary Nasal Syphilis: Tertiary nasal syphilis is the most easily overlooked in clinical practice, and various dangerous lesions also mostly occur during this stage. This is also the period of what is commonly called "opening the skylight" (開天窗). This stage mostly occurs one to three years after syphilis infection, or later, eight to fourteen years. At the beginning of tertiary nasal syphilis, the nasal mucosa mostly develops diffuse or localized swelling with increased secretion, easily breaking down and forming ulcers. The nasal cavity is filled with yellow, yellowish-brown, or greenish pus. If the pus is wiped away, a red and swollen mucosal surface can be seen. These ulcers have sharp edges, and their bottom surface is covered with a yellow, rouge-like substance. In the late stages, the nasal cavity becomes abnormally wide, and the walls of the nasal cavity are covered with green or brownish-green scabs with a foul odor. At this time, bone defects are commonly seen, or even necrotic bone fragments are exposed. This condition is called syphilitic ozena. The most easily affected part of the nasal cavity is the bony part of the nasal septum, followed by the nasal floor and roof. Therefore, the nasal septum often becomes perforated. If the upper anterior part of the perpendicular plate of the ethmoid bone or the lower end of the nasal bone develops ulceration and destruction, it can lead to a deformity of the external nose. Its shape resembles a saddle, so it is called a saddle nose. Sometimes, the disease progresses and is not treated. The nasal floor can be destroyed, and the palate can also be defective. During speech, there is often an open nasal sound. During eating, food and drink often flow backward into the nasal cavity. If the roof of the nasal cavity is also destroyed, it can cause meningitis and brain abscess, and other dangerous diseases. In addition, the patient themselves feels nasal obstruction, excessive secretion, a foul odor in the nose, easy scab formation, olfactory and gustatory disturbances, and pain in the head, nose, nasal bridge, forehead, and upper maxillary alveolar region.

Since nasal syphilis has the above-mentioned various dangerous lesions, we should be vigilant and not seek pleasure in brothels. If unfortunately infected with syphilis, we should seek medical treatment quickly and implement anti-syphilis treatment. If the treatment is delayed, this disease can develop and cause lifelong regret, or even death.

Q&A on Dental Knowledge (22) 215

— Lin Jianxian

(Question 109) After the deciduous teeth erupt, how should children's oral hygiene be maintained?

Answer: After children's teeth erupt, because the food they eat consists of milk and soft foods, they easily adhere to the deciduous teeth and form a yellow coating. Therefore, medicated gauze or clean, disinfected cloth strips should be used to frequently wipe clean the area around the teeth. At the same time, the gums should also be rubbed frequently to strengthen the muscles and promote blood flow.

(Question 110) What are the dangers of children putting their hands or toys in their mouths?

Answer: Children's hands and toys are often stained with many germs and dirt. If they are put in the mouth, it is very easy to get infected. Therefore, children should be taught not to develop the habit of holding their hands and objects in their mouths. Also, children's hands should be washed frequently, and toys should be chosen that are non-toxic and easy to wash.

(Question 111) At what age can children be taught to brush their teeth?

Answer: When children reach the age of four or so, they should buy a small toothbrush with soft, fine bristles. First, parents should brush their teeth for them, and gradually teach them to brush their teeth themselves. They should be brushed every morning and after meals, and should be supervised frequently. The benefits of brushing teeth and the beauty of clean, white teeth should be explained to arouse children's interest. The development of this habit of brushing teeth is truly an endless benefit for life.

Spring and Autumn

Climbing Changbai Mountain 216

— (Lu Jusheng)

Ming Xing Jie, style name Bokun, also known as Kuntian, was a native of Yidu, Shandong. He was a Jinshi in the fifth year of the Longqing reign. He successively served as imperial censor, right vice minister of the Ministry of War, and Pacification Commissioner, with many military achievements. In the 25th year of the Wanli reign, the Japanese invaded Korea, and Korea appealed to China for help. Duke Xing was ordered to lead the army to pacify them. He was also a national hero. These two poems on climbing Changbai Mountain were written on his behalf, and their value can be imagined.

The mountain colors are vast, pressing down on the great wilderness,

Climbing up to take a look, my mood becomes exuberant and wild.

Wearing light fur and a relaxed sash, I reminisce about the shepherd Su Wu,

Holding a feather fan and wearing a turban, I am ashamed to be a military official.

The Central Plains can be seen in detail from here,

The surging rivers and seas evoke memories of twists and turns.

The Han people still have troubles with the Xiongnu,

Who will build a golden city ten thousand miles long?

Climbing mountains and facing the water doubles my sorrowful spirit,

Turning back to look at the Central Plains, my eyes are full of tears.

Who laments the affairs of the Han Dynasty amidst warhorses,

When will the weapons of war quell the dust of the barbarians?

Every commoner has a responsibility for the rise and fall of the country,

Commoners are also subjects of the empire.

Thunder and lightning shake, and sweet dew sprinkles,

Let all the trees face the warm spring sun.

Record of Exploring Plum Blossoms at the Shi Kefa Shrine in Yangzhou 217

— Wu Wencan

The morning snow had just cleared, and I was reading when a guest arrived, heavily cloaked, and said to me: "You have long had a fondness for plum blossoms, and the plum blossoms in Yangzhou are most abundant at the Shi Kefa Shrine. Now they are almost ready to bloom in the cold. Why not go and explore them together?" I happily agreed and went with him. We exited the north gate and walked several dozen paces to the Shi Kefa Shrine. Turning east and then north, we reached Plum Blossom Ridge and ascended it. I thought that with their iron-like branches and icy demeanor, they must have absorbed the essence of heaven and earth and stood out in the wilderness. However, the paths were overgrown, the branches were half-withered, and only a few trees were blooming. They were the few remaining after the ravages of war. Alas! Plum blossoms, as things, are solitary, lofty, and detached from the world, and should be able to avoid calamity. Yet they cannot even protect themselves in times of chaos. How can a virtuous man who stands alone and acts independently not fear? We sighed together for a long time, recalling when we came here in the past, we only saw strong trunks of varying heights, and jade-like blossoms arranged in rows. We inhaled their pure fragrance and admired their noble qualities. Amidst the icy snow, they naturally shone together with Shi Kefa's unwavering integrity and loyalty. We admired Shi Kefa, as if we faintly met him in the dim fragrance and sparse shadows. How could they be felled and damaged, leaving only a few cold plum blossoms, suppressed in the cold smoke? This is even more lamentable! However, Shi Kefa, at the time when the Ming dynasty was about to fall, supervised the troops in the Jianghuai region. Although there was internal strife in the court and the fierce generals rejoiced in their towns, he upheld his great integrity and never yielded despite repeated setbacks. Today, although only a few plum trees remain, they stand tall amidst the remains of chopping and felling, spreading their fragrance in the season of desolation. Their perseverance and righteousness, their stern air and upright nature, are mostly similar to Shi Kefa. Therefore, seeing the plum blossoms is like seeing Shi Kefa. Moreover, now that the Hu (Qing) dynasty has been overthrown and the temple has been rebuilt, Shi Kefa's loyal spirit must be greatly comforted. If the plum blossoms had knowledge, they would also bloom with their brilliance to fulfill Shi Kefa's aspirations. I will wait and see. So I lingered with my guest beneath them, forgetting to return until dusk. Suddenly, the wind and clouds changed color, dense mists gathered, and the air became biting cold. We could not stay any longer, so we linked arms and returned together.

Visiting Yan Guang's Tomb on Guest Star Mountain 218

— Shufan

Yuyao is the hometown of Yan Guang. Guest Star Mountain, located ten li northeast of the city, is where he was buried after his death. His enduring influence and legacy spread among the people are no less than the Fishing Terrace on the Tong River. To the west is bordered by the Qian River and Cao River, and to the southeast is bounded by towering mountains and the vast sea. In the past, when boats and carriages were not yet common, travel was difficult, and few people from other places ever came here. Even the people of the county had largely forgotten him because the sacrifices to him were not properly maintained. On a solitary peak thousands of feet high, in the setting sun, who asks about the weeds on the grave mound, how green they have grown? Although I was born and raised in this county, I regret that I lived almost two miles away from the mountain. For many years, no one took me there, and when I grew up, I wandered around the country. My long-cherished wish has remained unfulfilled for almost thirty years. Once, at the end of the year, I returned home from visiting relatives in the province, traveling down the Shun River. Light snow had just begun to fall, and the wilderness was vast. I saw a crystalline peak standing before me, towering like a pillar. It was Guest Star Mountain, where I had longed to roam in my youth, showing its imposing form in the snow. Therefore, I immediately dismissed the idea of visiting relatives and went straight to the mountain. A magnificent archway stood at the foot of the mountain, creating a solemn atmosphere. The paths between the fields were frozen and slippery, making it very tiring to walk. After three miles, I turned into Yan Family Village, where Yan Guang's descendants lived. They farmed and fished, maintaining the customs of the Han Dynasty. I learned that there used to be a Guest Star Hall in the village, built by Shi Hao when he was stationed in Yue during the Song Dynasty, but now no trace of it could be found. Alas, how desolate the records have become! I asked the villagers about Yanling's burial place, and they pointed to a place deep in the white clouds. I climbed up the green cliffs, and the north wind was fierce, yet sweat still soaked through my clothes. Sometimes, snow falling from the pine trees hit my head, making me feel particularly cool. The mountain path was as straight as a line. With each step, I had to use my hands for support, moving like a snake or a cripple. I was extremely exhausted. After about an hour, I reached the middle of the mountain. There was a spring called Huaqing, where Yan Guang used to wash his feet. Although there is no proof of this, Sun Yingshi of the Song Dynasty wrote: "East of the county, the river is sparkling, and the tides rise and fall with constant sound. This is the Ziling Shoal, where he first fished and roamed. Ten li northeast is a strange peak called Chen Mountain (i.e., Guest Star Mountain), where he lived and was buried after his death." Whether fishing or living there, how could Yan Guang not have sung the song of the Canglang by this spring? After another four hundred paces to the east, the slopes leveled out, and a vast open space appeared. A mound of earth rose faintly, which I suspected was where Yan Guang was buried. However, there was no sealing or planting, so there was no way to identify it. Fortunately, the Gaofeng Pavilion on the left of the tomb stood majestically, providing mutual verification. The county gazetteer states: "The Gaofeng Pavilion is located to the left of Yan Ziling's tomb on Guest Star Mountain." Lou Yao of the Song Dynasty also wrote a poem: "The Fishing Terrace on the rocky shoal is not the old place, but the clouds and mountains and river waters are the Gaofeng." This means that the pavilion is the remains of the pavilion, and the thousand-year-old lacquer lamps can certainly be found among the desolate weeds. But after hundreds of years, the pavilion has collapsed and the tomb has been leveled. Who will come here to pay their respects? It is now the urgent duty of the people of the county to rebuild it. As dusk fell and I passed through the clouds, the valley winds howled on all sides. Looking straight to the north, the mountain was only a trace of green. I seemed to hear the ancient soul in the sky saying: "How can one dream of sheepskin robes and vast marshes in this day and age?"

Record of an Adventure in Jinzhu Stream 219

— Yi Liu

Among the scenic spots of eastern Zhejiang, Yandang Mountain is the most famous, and among the wonders of Yandang Mountain, Jinzhu Stream is the most outstanding. Its famous sites from the Six Dynasties period and Xie Lingyun's inscriptions have long attracted attention. However, in the past, the roads were rough and unexplored, so even those who traveled to Yandang Mountain did not see it, let alone Jinzhu Stream. When I arrived at Yandang Mountain with surprise, I first went to Nengren Temple. The temple monk Kehua was an old acquaintance, and he found a local villager named Cai Huangshouchun to be my guide. This man was quite unusual, literate and knowledgeable. When I asked him about the itinerary, he said that those who visit Jinzhu Stream must go by the stream and return by the mountain, so that they can fully appreciate its wonders in both directions. However, going by the stream is extremely dangerous, and not everyone can endure it. Many people give up halfway. If that is the case, it is better not to go at all. If you go, you must be determined to enjoy it to the fullest. Can you take the risk? I am willing to be your pioneer. I readily agreed and followed him, with walking sticks in hand. After entering the stream for four or five li, there was gradually no path. We walked in the stream, the rushing water boiling beneath our feet. The current was very rapid, and the rocks were as round as eggs. If we lost our footing, we would fall into the stream. So we ran left and right, suddenly changing direction. Before long, we came to a narrow gorge. The pool at the entrance of the gorge was large, and the sound was like thunder. The rushing water flowed straight down, and the bottom was a wide, smooth surface with no rocks to hold our feet. The guide carried me on his back and waded into the middle of the stream. The current became deeper and faster, almost reaching our knees. The stones were as slippery as grease. If we moved our feet forward slightly, we would lose our balance and fall. I was greatly frightened and cried out. The guide struggled to stand firm and moved forward slowly, step by step. We were soaked to the bone, and after catching our breath, we continued forward. The pool gradually became deeper, and the scenery became more secluded and beautiful. In the deep mountains, there were no people, and the sound of zithers was heard on the rocks. The poetic realm unfolded infinitely. After passing this point, deep pools and huge waterfalls appeared one after another. First was Lower Pei Pool, then Juying Pool. The water was deep blue, and the pool covered several acres. After another half a mile, we came to Lianhuan Pool, which was the most spectacular. The water flowed down from the upper end in a wide chute, passing through a narrow channel and flowing into a wide pool below. The stone wall was not deep, only about waist-high. At the bottom of the pool were two small pools, appearing in the shape of double wells, like a pair of eyeglasses. The water was dark blue, quite different from the outer pool. Looking down from above, the distinction was clear and distinct. Further on was the main branch of Jinzhu Stream. A huge waterfall roared in front of us, and we knew there was a steep current. Looking closely, we saw a large waterfall plunging down like a swimming dragon hanging upside down. The current was extremely fast. Below was a pool called Lotus Bearing Pool, which was particularly deep and wide, several times larger than the previous pools. The light on the water changed endlessly, from white to blue to green. We were filled with awe of the deep abyss. We held onto the rocks on the side and moved forward. The cliffs were sheer and endless, with no moss and no steps. We had to crawl forward, not daring to look to the side. Our hearts trembled and we were about to fall. With great effort, we finally reached the other shore, sweating profusely. The guide exclaimed: "It is not easy to cross here. From here on, it is all rocky paths, so you can rest assured." Looking back at the opposite side of the pool, we saw the full view of the waterfall, which was even more magnificent, with a chilling, ghostly atmosphere. It turned out that we had not seen its full form when we were passing behind it. Turning back, we faced a pool shaped like a sheep's kidney, with thick ends and a narrow middle. Above was a broken cliff, hanging down into the pool, a few feet from the surface of the water. Vines and creepers hung down with colorful flowers, reflecting in the water with the blue sky. When the wind rose, it washed the pool, striking the rocks and making a metallic sound, like the tinkling of jade pendants. It was named Qiangjin Pool, a fairy scene not of this world, surpassing all others. We were mesmerized for a long time. The guide urged us to move on. Another pool appeared before us. A slender waterfall washed the stream wall, and the sound of the water striking the stones was peculiar, like pearls splashing. It was called Shuyu Pool, secluded and deep, untouched by humans. Even the apes and birds were silent. We suspected that the monsters of the water were spying on us from below. The guide said: "It is now fifteen li from Nengren Temple. We have seen almost all the sights of Jinzhu Stream. If we go further, we will reach a fork in the road where we can return." So we climbed up the high mountain and returned.

This newspaper recently initiated group travel to adjust the lives of colleagues and enhance service efficiency. The first event was held the other day, with forty employees participating. They took an early train to Wuxi, hired a boat to tour the scenery of Taihu Lake, and thoroughly enjoyed sights such as Yuantouzhu, Meiyuan, and Liyuan. The picture above shows the Jieqiao bridge spanning Wuli Lake, which is about a mile long and has a majestic presence, adding much to the beauty of the lakefront (photographed by Bozhou).

A Trip to Xiang Lake in Xiaoshan 220

— Li Jiefei

On a day when the accumulated gloom had just cleared, and the universal light was clear and white, I awoke after a long sleep and felt a strong urge to travel. I hurriedly accompanied Mr. Wang Hong, and we boarded a bus at Guanxiangkou to the Jiangbin Sanlangmiao (Three Shrines) area. We switched from land to water, and the journey was about to begin.

The boat was newly painted, and there were few passengers. Looking around inside, there was ample space. It was the first month of the year, and the morning light was fresh and delicate, reflecting the peaks of Yuhuang (Jade Emperor) and other mountains to the south, like celestial beings in golden robes, suddenly appearing. The shadow of the Six Harmonies Pagoda resembled a large embroidered screen, lined with red silk, dazzling and eye-catching. The river water was clear and blue, shimmering like jade, with ripples resembling fish scales. This scene will be unforgettable for life. After half an hour, we arrived at Wenyan, a large town on the south bank of the Qiantang River. The residents were mostly boatmen, and the men were all out riding the tides, while the women were engaged in making paper foil. The streets were narrow, and the goods traded were mostly southern products, bamboo, wood, sugarcane, tangerines, and the like. We rested at the Xiang'an Central Elementary School. Even on their day off, the teachers and students were still discussing the "little teacher" system, which was very gratifying.

A little further on, we arrived at the Xianghu Zhejiang University Agricultural Farm. The surrounding area was all mountains, and the lake had been silted up to make fields. Further on was the training center for agricultural cooperative personnel. After walking around for an hour, we invited Mr. Yanmen to talk about local education. Standing below Ding Mountain, we looked at the pond water like a basin, the remains of the lake. The shape of the lake resembled a gourd, with the Kuahu Bridge in the middle, connecting the two banks. Ding Mountain and Yahu Mountain are both located in Upper Xiang Lake. In spring, they frequently offer rice shoots, and in summer, they sing about picking lotus roots. Perch and bayberries are produced in large quantities every year. There are also many historical sites along the lake, such as Tiger Cave, Yue King City, and Yilan Pavilion. Unfortunately, I could not visit them all. Further on was Yaohu Mountain, shaped like Xiaogushan (Little Orphan Mountain) in the Yangtze River, standing proudly and independently, surrounded by floating reeds. The Xianghu Normal School was located on the southern slope of the mountain, with male and female students bustling about, studying books and practicing arts, and experiencing life practically. Although life was simple and hard, it was of the highest quality. Extremes must be reversed, and reason dictates it. The division between those who labor with their minds and those who labor with their bodies has been erased in theory, and the realization of a return to the original model is now an urgent task of the times.

We had a simple meal of vegetables and water at the school. Although I have never been extravagant, I often wasted food in the past, far more than what I was consuming here. In the afternoon, we went to Xiaoshan, walking through the scenery of streams and fields, with mulberry and chestnut trees everywhere, and the sound of bamboo rustling in the wind. Having lived in the city all day, I felt like I was returning to my hometown when I took a walk in the countryside. Every tree and every patch of moss filled me with pure pleasure. The stone paths were narrow and winding, but full of charm. The villagers were content with their fields, and the women were diligent in making paper foil. We passed three or four Guandi (God of War) temples along the way. The spirit of fortitude, not seen in the capitals of Yan and Zhao, was evident in this gentle region, which was both gratifying and sad.

Record of Viewing Clouds on Lushan Mountain 221

— Wang Minji

It has been five months since I left Lushan Mountain, and what I miss most is the clouds of Lushan. The clouds of Lushan cannot be appreciated by those who seek summer refuge in Guling, nor can they be admired by tourists who ride in "four-man sedan chairs." Rather, it is by gazing at the panoramic view of Lushan in the morning light, in the twilight, in the midst of fierce winds and torrential rains that one can see this spectacle. These conditions naturally qualify fishermen and farmers, and I, a soldier, only occasionally get to feast my eyes. Su Shi's "Record of Stone Bell Mountain" says: "Scholars and officials will never be willing to moor their small boats at night under the steep cliffs, so they cannot know it. Fishermen and boatmen, though they know it, cannot express it. This is why it is not passed down in the world." I think the clouds of Lushan are probably buried for this reason.

Generally speaking, places with good scenery combine the beauty of mountains and water. The mountains of Lushan are steep, and naturally form many waterfalls. Silver rivers and white ribbons cascade down thousands of feet, almost everywhere you look. The Poyang Lake and Sha Lake at the foot of the mountains, the fishing boats, the water birds, and the sea of clouds where the water and sky meet, all give poets endless inspiration for impromptu verses about Lushan. Moreover, they provide a large amount of water vapor, which condenses into the magnificent sight of white clouds.

On sunny days, a thin layer of white clouds surrounds the mountainside, not connected to each other, like warships sailing in formation. Sometimes they are closely connected, and a white ribbon locks in those who enjoy themselves on the famous mountain. Sometimes they scatter into wisps of smoke, perhaps the "empty city plan" of the poor people at the foot of the mountain who have no rice to cook? When it is "drizzling and raining, without clearing for months," the entire Lushan disappears. In the depths of the white clouds, one or two solitary peaks occasionally emerge, appearing and disappearing, and one does not know whether the peaks are inserted into the clouds or the clouds cover the peaks! When it is about to clear up, the white clouds gradually converge, moving from whole to part, very leisurely and free, like cotton wadding or willow catkins. Sometimes they spread over the graceful and solitary peaks, like a young girl after bathing, how charming!

The best time is a clear morning, when the east is a fish-belly color, gradually conveying red light and shining on the changing, moving clouds, giving them a layer of rouge color, red, yellow, light yellow, decorating them into a natural watercolor painting. Clusters of red flowers cover the dense forests, cliffs, and waterfalls. Who can tell the difference between the red leaves of late autumn and the red flowers of February?

Once, we climbed Guling and, upon reaching the mountainside, we felt like we were in another world. The affectionate clouds stubbornly entangled us. We could not see the sky above or the ground below. We were already in the depths of the white clouds. Upon reaching the summit, our clothes were completely soaked. A gust of wind was mixed with a strange air, not raindrops, not fog, not even smoke. There was a cold, piercing chill, some moisture that could be felt but not seen. This was the clouds of Lushan, and what the ancients called the misty rain of Lushan.

Another time, we climbed Five Old Men Peak and were overlooking the surrounding scenery when suddenly a mass of white clouds rose leisurely from the mountain gorge, flying over our heads. A refreshing air that could be smelled washed away our vulgarity. I wanted to pick a piece off, but I was afraid of breaking up its companions. A companion was stunned and repeatedly chanted, "Misty rain of Lushan, Zhejiang tide."

On many steep cliffs, one can see bursts of cloud shadows. The sunlight shining from the clouds is also taken away by the cloud shadows in bursts. Sometimes the cliffs are covered with cloud shadows, and a strong ray of sunlight shoots out from the cloud shadows, reminding one of the taste of a film breaking in a low-class cinema.

The clouds of Lushan are beautiful and ever-changing. "We cannot recognize the true face of Lushan, only because we are in this mountain." I think the true face of Lushan is the clouds of Lushan!

Talks

Further Discussion on "Birth Control" 233

— Chui

I want to write a talk, but I can't find a topic. I have no choice but to talk about birth control again.

Jin Shengtan said, if you want to kill it, then don't give birth to it. If you want to give birth to it, then don't kill it. Zhou Gongying said, since you gave birth to [whitespace], why did you give birth to Liang? Fate makes fools of people, generally speaking. Therefore, Lao Tzu said, heaven and earth are ruthless, treating all things as straw dogs. Some people have property but no sons, while others have no property but many children: eldest, second, third, fourth, fifth, sixth… So when a baby is born, it must cry loudly first. There is real reason to it.

I strongly agree with Mrs. Sanger's advocacy of "birth control." I strongly oppose opposing Mrs. Sanger's advocacy of "birth control." If you don't believe me, let's discuss the reasons for opposing Mrs. Sanger one by one. The other day, there was an argument that "good elements practice birth control, while inferior elements give birth," which I discussed the other day. Now let's discuss two problems with "birth control."

Some say, "Although cities in China now feel densely populated, the rural border provinces are not densely populated. Ningxia has an average of only one person per square kilometer, Qinghai only one to three people, and Xixia only one to six people. Under these circumstances, advocating "birth control" is certainly wrong." I also say that advocating "birth control" in these places is wrong. In these places, not only should we not advocate "birth control," but we should also encourage childbirth like Hitler in Germany and ban singlehood. So I will definitely not advocate inviting Mrs. Sanger to Ningxia, Qinghai, and other places to spread her doctrine.

Or some may say that multiplying children in flourishing cities and sending them to Ningxia, Qinghai, and Xixia to develop those areas one day, isn't that the same? But we should know that the national character of our country tends to be settled, and the concept of territory is very deep. Whether children from flourishing cities are willing to go to places like Xixia and Ningxia is still a problem. So, we should first clarify the way out, and then talk about birth control.

Some say that raising many children is truly painful, but Mrs. Sanger's method is wrong. We should advocate public child care. This is even more far-fetched. Under the current circumstances, is public child care absolutely possible? Even if it's not absolutely possible, is there even a fraction of a possibility? I think this kind of argument is not a valid reason to oppose "birth control."

However, there is a problem. Nature is dual, or even multilateral. If it's only one-sided, then naturally it can't be a problem. I once again invite those who oppose birth control to think of a few more grounded and practical reasons to put forward for discussion.

Children 234

— Ying Guangjun

I love the children, and the children love me too.

Every day, as it's about to dawn, they come to play, jump, make noise, and sing songs in the yard.

My lonely mood and my homesickness are all dispelled by them. As soon as I hear them running from afar, shouting, my spirit goes over.

They are so interesting in their midst. Some are wearing bright and dazzling new clothes, some have stains on their tattered clothes. Hands, faces, surfaces, dirty ones, clean ones also became proportional to the clothes. I certainly love the well-dressed and clean children, but I still love the poorly dressed and dirty children just the same, because I, as the teacher, love the children themselves, not the children's wealth or poverty.

In class, they all sit quietly in their seats, eyes staring blankly at the blackboard, mouths following me as they read. Their serious reading, without the slightest carelessness, is precisely where their innocence lies.

After a while, if I ask: "Is there anyone who can't read? Who can read?" those who can read will raise their hands high, and those who can't will lower their heads tightly, peeking at me with their eyes—they don't know how to hide their weaknesses, but this is a virtue.

The ten-minute break is when they are busy. Hearing the sound of footsteps on the stairs, I know that they have given me more to do. They come to complain: either A hit B, or B cursed A, followed by some witnesses, all talking at once. Sometimes, I settle the matter peacefully for them. Sometimes it is really impossible to deal with, and I can only gently slap them a few times on the palm of their hands.

"Will you dare to do it again?"

I asked in pursuit, and the beaten children said in unison:

"I dare not, I dare not."

Even if I beat them, they don't hate me. Instead, they love me. Seeing a letter on the table that hasn't been sent, they ask to do their duty to do it for me. Seeing that there is no water in my kettle, they go to fetch water without getting my permission. Seeing me with nothing to do after class, it's time for them to ask me to tell a story. They love to hear stories, even more than they love listening to me talk about books in class. I tell them the history of "Reynard the Fox" and "Andersen's Fairy Tales." They often listen so intently that they don't want to go home for dinner.

Sometimes, they automatically propose to me, saying:

"Teacher, would you like me to tell you a story about a mouse stealing oil?"

"Teacher, let me tell you a fool's story."

"No, teacher, this story is about a 'Talking Foreign Doll.'"

I let them tell it in order of their names, but after saying a few sentences, they can't continue. They think, the more they think, the less they can say.

"I can't do it, I can't remember."

The other children all laugh. The storyteller turns red and hides behind people.

Only children are innocent and straightforward.

I really love this group of children. Whenever they are not in front of me, I feel restless. I am afraid of Sundays, I am afraid of every night. These are the moments that make me feel lonely and empty because I have lost them.

The other day, Tan Laosan went out wearing a small red hat. His yellow-faced wife said, "I'm afraid you have a red influence." He based it on this. Tan laughed and replied, "What about the red National Emblem all over the place?"

The Shanghai Telephone Company promulgated new charging regulations. The Special Zone Telephone Problem Committee sent representatives to negotiate, but there was no result. Users are waiting for the removal. Tan Laosan said, "It saves the trouble of listening to the phone and saves the cost of the phone. It's really killing two birds with one stone."

Early Winter in Qingyang Port (7) 236

— Qiu Yuan

Zhuo Min began writing her letters, and she immediately sent many provocative replies: she had visited Zhuo Min's old home in H-land, and she had him... In Zhuo Min, how could he stop his own love, his love for Qiu Hua. Although he was already a married man, although he was not a man who had no romances before, he always felt that he and Qiu Hua were unprecedented. It can also be said that this was his first love. Not only was it unprecedented, it was also unparalleled. He now knew that love should have this kind of charm. His previous view that there was only sex but no love now seemed ridiculous to him. He began to feel that although love is based on sex, it transcends sex at the same time. The attraction of sex cannot be considered the entirety of love, there should be a higher part of it.

In a clean guest room decorated with many oil paintings, after looking at many paintings, talking for many days, and drinking some foreign wine that the host treated with generosity, it was already somewhat cloudy when they left Mr. T's home. Walking into a store, sitting across from each other in a delicately small room, looking at Qiu Hua's curly hair, flexible eyes, and her intelligent demeanor, streetcars driving past the window were thinking, thinking.

--These public buses are all empty, you see.

--Yes, empty, empty. Zhuo Min replied in a slow tone.

"Empty are the public buses, but is emptiness not life itself, if there is no love?" Zhuo Min thought to himself, without saying a word. The waiter brought in hot dishes one after another, and poured wine into the glass—that beautiful Tianjin Wujiapi, as lovely as a beauty's lips. Each person drank several glasses, and was a bit tipsy.

Insulted and Humiliated 237

— Hong Ying

The night was as dark as ink. The street was languid and quiet. I was just about to go home from Botak Square, passing by the road called Sac Street behind the Rosa Li District Church. This [whitespace], saying it is a quiet [whitespace] is really so, saying it is a remote [whitespace] is also so, with low houses, thin sandy [whitespace] roads, filled with gloom and dullness.

I lowered my head and took slow steps, gently whistling to not feel lonely. When I whistled an American marching song, I was suddenly absorbed by a desolate sigh. It was so long and fragile that it seemed as if someone was gently exhaling near my ear. But when I stopped and listened [whitespace] attentively, it floated far away again, weak and quiet.

I was suspicious and felt a little scared. But I didn't believe that any ghosts were at work. On the top of the church was solemnly standing the sparkling cross. I looked up at it, gently drew a cross on my chest, and started whistling the American marching song, striding forward. I tried to take as many steps as possible, whistling regardless, just to pass this cursed place…, but my attempt failed. Before I had taken six or seven steps, that terrible long and fragile sigh came again. It was still so bleak and clear that I was almost surprised that it was following me closely. However, I was timid. I didn't have the courage to turn back to look behind me. I imagined that a large group of ferocious and hungry ghosts were following me. So I looked at the sparkling cross on the top of the church even more often, drew the sign of the cross on my body, and whistled loudly. But none of this worked, a miserable failure. I was deeply absorbed by a strange phenomenon. I discovered a gray-white monster shivering, and the dull sigh came from there.

I was shocked and stopped. I thought: this sounds like a person's voice, but why am I being urged to recognize it in such a late hour? So I quietly stepped closer to this gray-white monster.

This gray-white monster gradually became clear to me. I discovered a long hair, and a white shirt, followed by a body curled up like a scared pangolin. It was kneeling on the steps outside a stone room, holding its head tightly with both hands, and its whole body was trembling gently. It didn't seem to have noticed my presence yet, so I coughed deliberately, and stomped my feet loudly on the sandy ground. After a while, it raised its head. Two sharp eyes, a delicate nose, hair scattered messily, covering its entire cheeks. From this, I knew it was a young woman. She looked at me blankly for a while, and then, as if suddenly frightened, her whole body trembled, she raised her hand to me, and timidly cried: In the name of God, leave me! And put her head in her arms.

I hurriedly took a step back. When I looked at her carefully, I realized that she was naked. Her upper body was only covered with that small shirt, and her lower body was completely naked. This made me feel interested, so I said: No, miss, in the name of God, you can't refuse my help. I believe you must be an unfortunate and insulted person…, (to be continued)

Drama 238

Thunder and Lightning Drama Society

Transportation (1300) 6:00 PM to 7:00 PM

Director: Chen Yi

Cast:

Stepan Stepanovitch Chubukov... Ma Ling

Ivan Vassilevitch Lomov... Lin Fei

Natalia Stepanovna... Chen Xiang

The Proposal

Life is full of contradictions, hypocrisy, selfishness, and self-interest. Everyone lives in this circle. In this play, Chekhov's "The Proposal" reflects a real society. It unfolds as a comedy:

Ivan Vassilevitch Lomov is a young landowner in love with Natalia, the daughter of his neighbor Stepan Stepanovitch Chubukov. One day, Ivan, dressed in formal attire, visits Stepan, his main intention being to propose to Natalia in person.

Stepan, hearing Ivan stammer out his intention to propose to his daughter, is overjoyed and immediately calls Natalia out, telling them to talk face to face!

However, upon seeing Natalia, Ivan doesn't immediately propose, and their conversation leads to a dispute over a piece of land called "Oxen Meadows"! Ivan claims it was passed down from his ancestors, while Natalia insists it was passed down from hers. She claims it belongs to her and calls her father, Stepan, to prove it. The father agrees that it belongs to them. Unable to resolve the issue immediately, they engage in a mutually vicious and sarcastic conflict. Natalia, extremely angry, tells Ivan to get out. Ivan, overwhelmed by the insults from the father and daughter, runs out of the house in a panic!

She sits on an easy chair, gasping for breath, and waits for her father to tell her that Ivan came to propose. Hearing that he came to propose, she jumps up and immediately forces her father to call Ivan back.

Ivan runs back into the house for the second time. She immediately tells Ivan that the "Oxen Meadows" belong to him, but doesn't immediately bring up the proposal. Suddenly, they start arguing again, this time because Ivan says his hunting dog, "Ugadai," is better than Natalia's hunting dog, "Otkatai." She says his "Ugadai" is old and bad, like a worn-out horse, while he says her "Otkatai" can't catch foxes and only bullies lambs. He says he wouldn't trade five "Otkatai" for one "Ugadai"! Unable to resolve the issue, they again engage in cold and sarcastic insults. She again calls her father to prove whose dog is better. But the father says Ivan's hunting dog is too old and has too short a nose. Ivan, hearing this, becomes so angry and heartbroken that he faints and dies!

Stepan, seeing Ivan seemingly dead, panics and wants to kill himself with a pistol. But in a moment, Ivan miraculously wakes up! At this moment, Stepan immediately takes his daughter's hand and Ivan's hand and forcefully says, "She agrees! Quick, kiss!"

Indeed, Ivan and Natalia immediately embrace and begin to kiss. Although in a sweet and long kiss, she can't help but say, "Ugadai" is bad! Bad! Bad! He says: Good! Good! Good!

At this moment, Stepan loudly and forcefully shouts, "The happiness of the family begins, bring the champagne!"

The comedy "The Proposal" closes in the shout of "Bring the champagne!"

Opening "New Daiyu Buries Flowers"

Today I bury the withered flowers, who will bury me in the future? Thinking of this, her heart aches again. She bids farewell at the tomb and returns to Xiaoxiang. In later years, she will burn the manuscripts and her fragrant soul will scatter, like fallen flowers drifting back to the wilderness. Although the beauty is dead, her name is praised.

"Incarnation Girl" Play within a Play 244

— Fang Lang

Yesterday, "Incarnation Girl" was filming a scene in which Yuan Meiyun returns from Nanyang to visit her ancestral home. Unexpectedly, a big joke occurred, which was both humorous and witty. I hereby record it to entertain everyone.

The plot of this scene involves Wang Guilin, who plays Yuan Meiyun's grandfather, receiving a telegram from his son Jiang Xiu, saying that the ship will arrive at the port on a normal day. He is overjoyed and hurriedly sends the servants to prepare a banquet to welcome his son Jiang Xiu, who has returned from abroad, and his grandson Yuan Meiyun, whom he has never met. However, Yuan Meiyun's cousin, Han Lingen, is extremely greedy and steals food, often suffering from diarrhea due to overeating. On this day, the scene being filmed was Han Lingen stealing food. In advance, director Fang Peilin had specially asked the props department to buy a dollar's worth of bananas and place them on the table. When the scene started, Han Lingen's gluttony and strange expressions while stealing bananas were all captured on camera. After several takes, there were very few bananas left on the table, and the banana peels were scattered all over the ground. At this time, Fang Peilin became a little worried and asked Han Lingen if eating like this would really make him sick. Han Lingen? He patted his chest, raised his thumb, and said, "Even if there's another dollar's worth, don't worry about it..."

Because he had said that, everyone didn't worry about it, and the scene proceeded smoothly. When they were filming Wang Guilin discovering Han Lingen stealing bananas and flying into a rage, Han Lingen's comical expression caused laughter throughout the studio. Unexpectedly, an interesting thing happened, making all the staff laugh so hard that they leaned forward and backward, and even tears flowed. That is, Han Lingen really ate something bad and his stomach started hurting, he ran into the toilet in such a panic, holding his stomach.
